Investigation Record of Dike Construction in the Bandit Area (II) 152

The Seventh District Construction and Relief Bureau's project, the south bank of the Yangtze River, from Tashi Station in Huarong County to Majiayuan in Shiyuan, the north bank from Guanyin Island in Jianli County to Tuomaobu in Jianli County, so the Yangtze River dike project from Zhenjiang to Jianli has reached its end. The Eighth and Ninth Districts belong to the Xiang River basin. On the evening of the 7th, on the way back to Hankou from Jianli on the Wan'an wheel, after dinner, a meeting was held in the restaurant as usual. Xi Dejiong, director of the Construction and Relief Office, invited people from the press to talk about their opinions after inspecting the dike project. The crowd elected Qian Hua to deliver a speech, saying that it was a great honor for the comrades to participate in the group invited by the Water Disaster Association, and that they were very grateful for the special reception and various conveniences along the way. Regarding the dike project, the Yangtze River has been seen from afar, and the greatness of the project and the hard work and dedication of the members of the Water Disaster Association and the Construction and Relief Office, who have completed this 15,000-mile long dike in the shortest time and with the least amount of funds, are admirable. The work in the bandit area is even more difficult. Today, the comrades have experienced it firsthand, and feel the danger and difficulty of the work at that time. Therefore, the completion of this great project is enough to show the spirit of our Chinese nation uniting to save itself and bravely resisting disasters. I hope that the members of the Water Disaster Association will continue to serve the country with this valuable spirit of struggle. We must know that China is now in turmoil, and the brutality of foreign oppression is a hundred times greater than last year's flood. The life of the nation is in danger. I hope that you will guide the people with the spirit of saving the flood and building a 10,000-mile dike, and take responsibility together. The members of the press are very willing to follow you and work together to deal with foreign aggression. The revival of China can be hoped for.

Honghu Base Area 153

The red bandits in Hubei are most famous for He Long's troops in the central Hubei area. He Long took Honghu as his base, which was recovered by the Tenth Army in September of this year. Hua Wenxuan, commander of the 5th division, who took the Wan'an wheel to Jianli, actually participated in the previous and subsequent battles. According to Hua, Honghu was the seat of the Soviet government of the Xiang-E-Xi province, and the facilities were relatively complete. There were armories, wounded soldier hospitals, prisons, Lenin schools, mints, and military academies, as well as a Lenin warship and two airplanes. Although the scale was very small and the machinery was very simple, there was still considerable output every day. The important organs of the red bandits were all underground. A large hole was dug in the ground, covered with wood and grass, and the structure was strong to prevent attacks by the national army's aircraft. A post office was also set up in the bandit area, with red stamps, one side with Lenin's image and the reverse side with a sickle and axe, and the Soviet silver dollars used were also the same. The bandit soldiers wore black uniforms. When they captured cities, the looted property had to be handed over to the bandit government and deposited in the Agricultural and Industrial Bank. The copper coins obtained were distributed to the soldiers for use. Soldiers and civilians were not allowed to hoard silver dollars worth more than three yuan. Except for the special affairs officers and quartermasters in the battalion, no foreign currency was named. The red bandits paid great attention to propaganda. Slogans were posted everywhere, and there were countless kinds of them. This was especially true during wartime. There were newspapers such as the Red Flag Newspaper and Weekly War Reports. The effectiveness of the propaganda was greatest in the winter of the year before last and the spring of last year. Even seducing the army everywhere, and using women to lure them, so at that time, suppressing bandits was only a name, but in fact, there was no battle. The wounded soldier hospital was empty. Later, the true colors of the red bandits were revealed, the propaganda lost its effectiveness, and it finally failed. All the strong men in the bandit area were forcibly conscripted, and a committee for desertion was set up. When a certain place was defeated and abandoned, the committee led the entire village of men, women, and children to flee, with only a few disabled people left behind. ㈠ To prevent the leakage of various military news in the bandit area, ㈡ To cause food shortages in the areas occupied by the national army. The bandits had four kinds of slogans for dealing with the national army's plans: ㈠ You go, I chase, ㈡ You station, I go, ㈢ You chase, I avoid, ㈣ You avoid, I attack, which is what the art of war says, avoid the real and attack the emptiness. The national army has been suppressing bandits for years, but has never succeeded. This is the reason. When the Tenth Army attacked the bandit nest in Honghu, many prisoners were captured, including many members of the false provincial government. Most of the houses were burned by the bandits, and the old, weak, and women who returned successively temporarily built thatched sheds to live in. The desolation was full of sight and could not be restored in a few years. The bandits were most well-informed about the news of the national army. There were many telegraph and telephone specialists. Most of the confidential telegrams sent by the national army were stolen. The recent theft of the headquarters' confidential telegram book was also related to the red bandits. I once searched for the diary of an important bandit leader in the Honghu nest of the red bandits. The phone reports of our side during the war were recorded in the book in detail, without any difference. This is also the work of the telephone worm. Whenever a stranger entered the bandit area, there was intelligence from all sides, reporting to governments at all levels for close surveillance. Strangers and villagers were not allowed to talk directly, otherwise they would be charged with counter-revolution. Therefore, it was almost impossible for the national army's detectives to inquire. The villagers feared the bandits like tigers. Even after the bandit army was defeated, they dared not tell the truth when the national army inquired, for fear of the bandits coming again. The reporter inquired about the situation of the red bandits from the village elders in the bandit area, but they always spoke vaguely. If asked firmly, they said it was still good. Under the accumulated power, it is really difficult for the common people. After arriving in Jianli, the headquarters' Recovery of Disaster Area Rural Financial Relief Office landed and went to Honghu, Qianjiang, and other places to conduct on-site investigations of agriculture and forestry. The reporter wanted to go with them, but due to time constraints, he could not do so, which was a great pity.

Strategies for Bandit Area Relief 154

The reporter returned to Hankou from Jianli and met a certain military authority, who said that the reasons for suppressing the red bandits this time were: ㈠ Chiang, the military chairman, sat in Hanzhong and concentrated the military forces of the three provinces, unified command, and launched an attack on the bandit area, making it impossible for the bandits to take care of each other. ㈡ Concentrate political talents to handle the aftermath of the bandit area. ㈢ The people in the bandit area all felt the deception of the red bandits and had automatically awakened. During the advance of the large army, they automatically organized a anti-communist volunteer team to assist the national army in searching for the remaining bandits in the area. ㈣ The three provincial armies attacked at the same time, which invisibly blocked the bandit area and cut off the bandits' food and other material supplies, making it impossible for the bandits to hold out for long. ㈤ The red bandits were divided internally due to the removal of the reform faction, and the mutual feuding greatly reduced their strength. As for the aftermath of recovering the bandit area, the following matters should be handled completely with political power, so that it can be a permanent solution and the red bandits will not relapse: ㈠ Actively organize volunteer teams in each county and village to consolidate the people's self-defense force, strictly enforce household registration investigations, and implement mutual guarantee and joint responsibility, so that the bandits have no place to hide. ㈢ Actively handle rural relief so that returning farmers have a livelihood. ㈣ After the household registration investigation is clear, immediately set up cooperatives to gradually stabilize the lives of farmers. ㈤ Appoint troops to build roads in designated areas to facilitate traffic in the bandit area and prevent the bandits from hiding. ㈥ Use political power to engage in production, transfer and introduce financial services. The Three Provinces Bandit Suppression Headquarters has now established a Disaster Area Rural Financial Relief Office to recover and for the restoration of farmland in the bandit area, and there are three methods: ㈠ Those who have deeds will return the original field. ㈡ Those whose deeds have been lost can also be returned with the testimony of the four neighbors or village elders. ㈢ Those whose deeds have been lost and no one can testify for them, the land will be managed by the Rural Revitalization Committee, and the benefits of hiring farmers to cultivate the land will be used for rural revitalization. In addition, there are loan relief measures, etc., which can be implemented one after another after the on-site investigation of the rural area is completed. (Sent by Qian Hua from Hankou on December 10)

Report of the Embankment Inspection Group 155

Ten Days of Observing the Embankment Works of the Yangtze River, Contributing Opinions on the Embankment Works of the Han River

The Embankment Inspection Group reported to Chairman Song, stating: "Respected Chairman Song of the National Government's Flood Relief Committee, upon receiving the telegram inviting inspection, the team inspected the Xujiawan Embankment in Jiujiang County on the morning of the 2nd of this month, and the Maqikou Embankment in Guangji County and the Chengzhen Embankment in Yangxin County in the afternoon. After arriving in Hankou on the 3rd, we inspected the flood control embankments along the river, as well as the Zhanggong Embankment and the Wujin Embankment in Wuchang. We found that Wuhan suffered the most severe damage during last year's flood. This time, your committee allocated grain to repair the embankments in sections, providing security for millions of lives, which is of great significance. On the 4th, we attended the tea party hosted by General Commander Chiang and the banquets hosted by the Hubei Provincial Government and the Hankou Municipal Government. On the afternoon of the 5th, we switched to the Wanan shallow-water vessel and sailed upstream to inspect the embankment works in the section from Jingkou to Huakou in Jiayu County. According to local statistics, since the construction of the embankment by the Work Relief Bureau, the area of farmland benefiting this year has exceeded one million mu. On the 6th, we inspected the Hujia Zhou Embankment in Mianyang County and the Yinjiatou and Zoumatou Embankments in Jianli County. On the 7th, we inspected the embankment works from Shangchewan to Jianli, walking thirty li. Many villages along the way were burned down by the Communist bandits. Although they have been recovered, the people have not yet fully returned, and it seems that relief for the refugees cannot be delayed. On the evening of the 8th, we returned to Hankou and stayed at the Yangtze River Hotel. In the past few days, all the embankments we passed through were within the scope of the Fourth, Fifth, Sixth, and Seventh Work Relief Bureaus. The width of the embankment surface is generally above eight meters, with an inner slope of one to three to one to five, and an outer slope also beyond one to three. The work is generally solid. According to local people, the personnel of the work relief bureaus entering and leaving the bandit areas have suffered greatly and have been killed. However, the workers have completed the work to the end, and their spirit of hardship and excellence is admirable. Moreover, the area from Wuhan westward in Hubei is mostly swamp, and the people rely on the embankments for protection. Therefore, the magnitude of the construction of the embankments far exceeds that of other places. However, residents inevitably build houses arbitrarily on the embankments or plant cotton and bean plants on the slopes. If this is not prohibited, it will inevitably affect the entire project. This is one point. The Hubei Water Conservancy Bureau has dumped stones in dangerous areas along the riverbank, but the paving is not entirely adequate. It seems that the Jianghan Engineering Bureau should be employed to repair them to prevent collapse. Also, the Yangtze River is particularly curved upstream from Hankou, especially in places like Paizhou, Luzhou, and Dama Zhou, where the straight-line distance is only a few miles, but the boat trip around is more than ten miles away. For the convenience of transportation and the protection of good farmland, it seems that these areas should be reorganized as soon as possible. This is the second point. Regarding the above two points, we propose that your committee forward them to the relevant agencies for special attention to benefit the people of Hubei. We plan to take the Han River route on the 10th to inspect the Han River embankment works managed by the Eighth and Ninth Districts. All the circumstances of the inspection of the embankment works from Hankou upstream to Jianli are hereby reported in advance for your review. Members of the Embankment Inspection Group: Wen Lanting, Zhou Xiangxian, Li Zu, Qian Hua, Lu Yi, Hu Chuanyuan, Zhu Yunguang, Pan Zeji, Chen Shizhang, Guo Wen, Wang Yinping, Stroeh Ford Frn-goh, etc., and all members, respectfully."

Protection Corps Members Imprisoned for Official Duties, All Protection Corps in Pudong Request Vindication 156

Yang Xialing, a member of the Tangqiao District Protection Corps in Pudong, shot and killed Jiang Guohua, a petitioning police officer from the Second District, who resisted arrest by firing a gun while being questioned as a suspect in July of this year. Recently, the local court suddenly detained Yang Xialing during the continued trial of the case, causing public outrage among the people of Pudong. The members of the district protection corps even wanted to resign en masse in support. All merchants in the district also believed that Mr. Yang was imprisoned for official duties and specially established a support association to provide unanimous assistance. In addition, all protection corps in the entire Pudong area also believed that Mr. Yang's detention was unfair and provided unanimous support. Mr. Zhang also believed that the corps member was imprisoned for official duties and should be rescued according to law. It was decided that the management committee would report to the municipal government and forward a letter to the court to release Yang Xialing on bail according to law to appease public anger. The submission is recorded below: "Presented: Corps members imprisoned for official duties, public anger is difficult to calm, and the corps is about to disintegrate. It is requested to present to the municipal government and forward a letter to the court to quickly grant bail, hoping for review. Corps member Yang Xialing must attend every hearing when summoned, and the court has granted bail. However, on the 8th of this month, corps member Yang was summoned to court and suddenly detained without bail. All corps members are about to stop winter defense immediately, and merchants are also terrified, and are starting to provide assistance together. Although the corps leader tried his best to persuade them to calm down, public sentiment is indignant, and it is impossible to quell without redress. If they lose heart, disintegrate, and stop defending, it will have a significant impact on local security. Honor of the Institute of Linguistics of the Academia Sinica

French Academy Awards This Year's Julien Prize 158

This newspaper published a Havavas dispatch from Paris, stating that a French society awarded a prize to the Academia Sinica. Upon inquiring with Mr. Yang Xingfo, the executive director of the Academia Sinica, about the details, Mr. Yang replied that this matter was seen in a cable from Paris this spring. The Academia Sinica did not know the details. Later, they received a letter from the Academy of Inscriptions and Belles-Lettres of the French Academy on March 5, stating that this year's Julien Prize was awarded to the Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica, partly because of the published collections and other related publications of the institute, especially the Anyang Excavation Report compiled by Li Ji and others. The prize money is a small matter, but it is gratifying that part of the work of the Academia Sinica has been praised by the national academic institution of a friendly country. The authority of the French Academy (Institut de France) in the world of academia is unparalleled. This is well known to the world. Among them, the Academy of Inscriptions and Belles-Lettres (Académie des Inscriptions et Belles-Lettres) is specifically responsible for ancient studies, linguistics, oriental studies, etc. Its position in ancient studies, linguistics, and oriental studies is also a leader. When asked about the work of the Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica, Mr. Yang said that the institute is divided into three groups. The first group is history, which is currently organizing the archives of the Ming and Qing dynasties' Grand Secretariat and studying classical texts, epigraphy, and northwest history and geography and Tibetan and Mongolian languages. The second group is linguistics, which studies phonetic experiments, investigates dialects, and organizes rhyme books. The third group is archaeology, which has excavated the Yin Ruins for eight seasons, and the results have attracted the attention and praise of most archaeologists in the world. It has also jointly established the Shandong Antiquities Research Association with the Shandong Provincial Government and has excavated Suoyitan City. It has also jointly established the Henan Antiquities Research Association with the Henan Provincial Government and is currently excavating Junxian, all of which have major discoveries. All the work and results of the institute can be found in the published publications of the institute, which have now been published in dozens of volumes and cannot be fully described here.

Whether the Skeletal Remains of the Female Ghost Are Human Is Still Unclear, Blood Stains Are Currently Being Tested... Expected to Be Completed by the End of the Month 159

The case of the female ghost discovered in Xianqin Temple in Yixing, which was once widely reported, has attracted attention from all sectors of society since the military stationed in the temple unsealed and excavated the skeletal remains and other items. It is understood that the skeletal remains have been examined and the blood stains are currently being tested. The entire process is expected to be completed within a month. Yesterday, someone took a car to the institute in Zhenru to investigate the details of the case. The details are recorded below.

The Beginning and End of the Case 160

Although everything has been repeatedly reported since the beginning of this case, it is still not completely clear. According to Lin Ji, the director of the Zhenru Forensic Institute, after the Fourth Regiment of the Provincial Security Infantry奉命 moved into Xianqin Temple outside the South Gate of Yixing, several rooms on the right side of the Prajna Hall in the backyard became the medical clinic, and one room on the left was used by the monks to store sundries, which was tightly sealed. The nurses in the medical clinic often stayed overnight, and some sick soldiers entered. At that time, there was often a crying sound in the empty room every night, and the sound was sharp. The soldiers were alarmed and ran away. The ninth company commander, Fan Zhengwen, reported the situation to Xu Qijin, the battalion commander of the Third Battalion, who went to investigate together and heard the crying sound. They became suspicious and, the next afternoon, supervised the monks and soldiers to open the door for inspection. They saw broken doors, windows, and tables and chairs piled up in the room, with blood-like stains inside. They then dismantled part of the floor and found a torn piece of clothing, socks, and pants. At this point, their suspicions grew stronger and they immediately reported to the unit by telephone, inviting representatives from the county government's public security bureau to the camp for a joint inspection. They found that part of the land in the inner corner was quite loose and supervised the soldiers to excavate more than a foot, first discovering a face towel with faint blood stains and the markings "Changjing". There was also a handleless kitchen knife and a plane, both covered in rust, and several large and small bones. They immediately took photos of the items found for storage and drafted a proposal outlining five suspicious points in the case, requesting the superiors and the county government to investigate. They also set up a planchette at night to ask the name of the murderous monk and the truth of the case. It was later revealed that the deceased was a woman from Xia Zhuang Bridge, and people were sent to Xia Zhuang Bridge to inquire, and it turned out that there was such a person, and a woman had indeed disappeared several years ago, and so on. This is the situation of the case.

The number of bones sent was very small, and there were only seven or eight teeth, so this institute took the investigation very seriously. Liu Chongwu and others, indignant that the general merchants in this city only know how to profit personally, sabotaging the boycott movement, and openly selling enemy goods, decided to deal with them by radical means. The Process of Arrest 165

At 2:30 p.m. on the 25th of last month, an assassination case suddenly occurred in house number 1040, Siwenli, Xinzha Road. One person, Wang Shouxi, was killed, and four people, including Cao Boqian, were injured. The murderer escaped from the scene. Afterwards, the Xinzha Police Station arrested two men and women, including Tang Zhangshi and Xu Runzhi, who were suspected of the case. The suspects confessed that the murderer, a tailor, was hiding at number 365, Hede Road. Inspector Zhao Bingkun and others went to arrest him, but the tailor had already fled. Inspector Zhao was afraid that he would return, so he waited there that day. At 6:30 p.m. on the 28th, Liu Chongwu entered from outside. Inspector Zhao felt that his actions were suspicious and arrested him. A loaded pistol was found on his body. He was then taken to the police station. At that time, a bombing case also occurred at the Deyuanchang Foreign Goods Store at number 567, Kangjiaqiao, Connaught Road. Police Officer Gu Xiang questioned him, and Liu immediately admitted that he had thrown the bomb. After repeated investigations, it was determined that although Liu had no connection with the assassination in Siwenli, he had participated in most of the cases in the concession where shops repeatedly selling Japanese goods received warning letters from a certain group, or were bombed, or even had shop employees injured by gunfire. He was immediately detained and, based on Liu's confession, the search began. On the morning of the 29th, Chinese and Western detectives went to the home of Pan Hongsheng at number 484, Guangdong Road, and arrested Pan. Later, Pan's younger sister, Huizhu, was also arrested. Huizhu led them to house number 40, Henan Road, where a loaded pistol was found. They then went to number 37, Wuhu Road, and arrested six Suzhou people, Cao Songshou, Tang Kang, Wu Ligang, Zhang Linxiang, Fan Xisheng, and Xu Weizu. Cao also confessed that a certain Gao, who lived at number 263, Tianjin Road, was also involved. When they went to arrest Gao, he had already fled, so they searched the house. Two pistols and some bullets were found on the roof. Cao also led the detectives back to his home and found a loaded pistol. Later, they went to number 13, Xingdeli, Laobeimen Street, and arrested Tian Shuiyang. On the 30th, detectives from the Huishi Police Station went to the Liangxi Hospital at number 728, Qipu Road, and seized letters related to the bombing case. They arrested the doctor of the hospital, Zhu Erkang from Wuxi. At the same time, Inspector Zhao arrested Hua Zhida from Wuxi at number 31, Xinzha Road. In three days, a total of twelve people were arrested, and five pistols, pistol bullets, rifle bullets, etc., were seized. Two of the guns were verified by the firearms inspection office as having been used.

▲The Cabin Was Full of Living Sheep Floating On the Sea

▲A Total of Eighty-Five Drowned

Steam Train Crashes into Workers' Train Near Tientong'an 175

▲ Fortunately, no one was killed

At approximately 5:15 PM yesterday, a workers' train departing from the Wusong Zhang Huabang Railway Factory of the Songhu Railway, while passing the Yangqi outside Xibaoxing Road near Tientong'an, stopped outside the Yangqi to wait to enter the station due to the blockage of Passenger Train No. 10 of the Jinghu Railway at the Shanghai Station. At this time, an upward passenger train (i.e., steam train) that departed from Paotaiwan at 4:25 PM for Shanghai arrived at Tientong'an Station. Unexpectedly, while traveling near Xibaoxing Road, the driver did not notice that there was still a workers' train stopped in front. By the time he noticed, the train was too close to brake, resulting in a violent collision with the workers' train. The front of the steam train was damaged, and the driver was injured. The compartment at the back of the workers' train was also completely destroyed. Passengers inside the steam train fell from their seats into the carriage, suffering head injuries, arm injuries, and severe shocks. Fortunately, the train was moving very slowly, so no one was seriously injured. After the accident, the passengers disembarked on their own and left. Continued Hearing of the Case Against Flood Relief Association Officials - The Case of Quan Shaowu 176

The issue of suspension of relief causes further complications; proceedings are temporarily suspended pending investigation of evidence.

Flood Relief Association officials Yang Shucheng, Quan Shaowu, Wang Fanwu, and Zha Liangzhao were accused by the Anhui Native Place Association in Shanghai to the First Special District Local Court for handling flood relief in northern Anhui. The details of the multiple trials have been reported in the newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Ting_ once again summoned both parties and witnesses for a continued hearing. However, the first accusation against the second defendant Quan Shaowu, regarding the suspension of emergency relief in Wuhe County, has not been concluded after two hearings. Therefore, the hearing focused on this accusation first. Quan Shaowu's lawyer stated that the plaintiff claimed that the defendant suspended emergency relief in Wuhe for fifteen days, from May 26 to June 9. The defendant had already submitted the stub of the relief ticket from May 29, proving that relief was not suspended. Yesterday, they submitted eleven booklets of ticket stubs from several days before and after May 29, which further proves that relief was not suspended. Judge Wu examined each of the submitted ticket stubs and noticed that the numbers were not consecutive between books. He then questioned Quan Shaowu in detail about the procedures for inspecting and distributing relief, as well as the reason for the discrepancy in ticket numbers. Quan explained each point and stated that this was a matter of procedure, and that these ticket stubs had already been reviewed twice. If there were any inaccuracies, the reviewing body would have reported them to the Flood Relief Association. Since there were no objections from the reviewers, it shows that there were no irregularities. Furthermore, the plaintiff is accusing the defendant of suspending relief; he requested that the hearing investigate whether relief was actually suspended. The plaintiff's representative, Li Zhenya, and the chairman of the Wuhe Relief Branch, Chen Shuizhen, successively refuted Quan's explanation of the relief distribution procedures and the non-consecutive ticket numbers. The plaintiff's lawyer also presented official documents from the Wuhe County government and sworn statements from several flood victims in Wuhe, all firmly stating that not only was there no relief distribution on May 29, but no relief committee members visited in the three days before or after May 29, so there was no relief distribution. Quan Shaowu argued that the distribution on May 29 was in cash, which was distributed by He Bingheng, sent by the Anhui Northern United Committee, and did not go through the local relief branch or the county government. The court pointed out that relief distribution must involve local personnel, so they questioned Quan about who distributed the cash. Quan replied that only He Bingheng knew this, but the relief tickets were still stored in Bengbu and could be inspected. The plaintiff's lawyer then presented the minutes of the Wuhe Relief Branch meeting, stating that at 9:00 PM on June 2, the relief branch invited the county magistrate, party committee, and chairman of the Chamber of Commerce to a meeting, and He Bingheng was also present. The minutes stated that He reported on the spot that he had brought 4,000 yuan in cash. Based on this, the earliest relief distribution would have started on June 3. However, Quan's lawyer also presented the Flood Relief Association's disbursement report, proving that the 11,000 yuan in relief funds for Wuhe had already been fully disbursed. At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer claimed that Wuhe only received 5,000 yuan, and the remaining 6,000 yuan was still missing, and that the plaintiff would need to add accusations against the defendant. This led to another complication, and the investigation into the suspension of relief could not continue. The court ordered a halt to the proceedings on this accusation and ordered further investigation of the evidence before resuming the hearing. The hearing then proceeded to the second accusation against Quan Shaowu, regarding the withholding of 75 tons of relief wheat from Xuyi County. According to Tan Shaohua, a relief committee member from Xuyi, the county was supposed to receive 300 tons of relief wheat, but only received 150 tons of relief wheat and the value of 75 tons of wheat, leaving a shortage of 75 tons. Although they had received the bill of lading, the wheat could not be retrieved. He presented the bill of lading as evidence. Quan Shaowu stated that the county was supposed to receive 300 tons, which had already been fully disbursed. He presented evidence such as the receipt issued by Xuyi County Magistrate Wang Xinlan. Both sides held to their own accounts and had substantial evidence. After repeated inquiries by Judge Wu, it was revealed that the 75 tons of relief wheat from the county had been collected in Mingguang by a Mr. Wang, because there was a guarantee from the local Chamber of Commerce, so the bill of lading was not collected. Furthermore, Tan Shaohua was aware of this matter and had written a letter to him. After the court presented the letter to Tan for review, he insisted that it was not his handwriting and requested to write a sample on the spot for comparison. However, it was late, and Judge Wu ordered the hearing to be postponed to another day.

National Federation of Chambers of Commerce Requests the Formulation of a Stamp Tax Law 178

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce yesterday sent a telegram to the Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry of the Nanjing National Government stating that they had received a letter from the Beiping Municipal Chamber of Commerce which roughly stated: "Upon investigation, the Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax of the Republic of China, drafted and promulgated by the former Ministry of Finance, are largely incomplete. At the time, because the Stamp Tax Law had not yet been formulated, the regulations were temporarily used as a substitute for the law to serve as a transition. However, since it is named 'provisional,' it implies temporary measures and should not be implemented for many years. Although stamp tax bureaus in various provinces and regions take advantage of the incompleteness of the law to facilitate fines, the original intention of legislation was to protect the rights of various deeds and personal certificates. It is not appropriate to deliberately set traps to trick people into them. Moreover, without clear written regulations, those with power have the advantage in determining right and wrong, and ordinary people have no recourse. Now, we list the points of extreme pain in the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations. In addition to the original text being on file and avoiding redundant narratives, we conclude by stating that since the capital of Beiping moved south, the market has become increasingly depressed, and corruption has become increasingly rampant. Thinking of this, we cannot help but shed tears. We earnestly request your association to forward this to the authorities and approve the request to address the points of pain mentioned above. First, provincial and municipal stamp tax bureaus should not arbitrarily impose fines. Urgently formulate a Stamp Tax Law, etc." Based on this, upon investigation, the incomplete clauses of the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations give unscrupulous officials the opportunity to seek personal gain and arbitrarily impose harsh fines. The association has previously received complaints from chambers of commerce in various provinces, counties, and cities, and the accumulated cases are voluminous, truly a source of widespread resentment. We have repeatedly telegraphed requests for the formulation of a Stamp Tax Law. Based on the letter above, we hereby telegraphically report to your government and departments for verification and approval. We earnestly request that you promptly order the Legislative Yuan to formulate a Stamp Tax Law and urge that provincial, county, and municipal stamp taxes not be arbitrarily imposed before the Stamp Tax Law is formulated, in order to alleviate the difficulties of businesses. We sincerely hope for this. Chairman Lin of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, Kanghou, respectfully submits this petition with a seal.

Commercial Corps Officer Retires and Returns Home 179

Captain J.W. Hincdcliffe

Reader's Advisor 180

A letter from Mr. Wang Zixin: "...I graduated from high school at the age of twenty-one. My grades in school were very good in all subjects. The teachers all said that I was a promising young man, and I myself felt that my future was bright. After graduation, because of family financial difficulties, I could not go to college. I was not disappointed, because I always thought that even if I could not go to college, I could find a suitable job by relying on myself. Sure enough, I relied on my pen to get into a certain company. The manager saw that my articles and handwriting were very good, so he assigned me to manage the documents. I was very happy to learn this, because I thought that this was my strength; because when I was in school, I often contributed to publications and served as the editor of the school newspaper for a year. The writing in this store is certainly easier. Unexpectedly, I ran into a snag the first time, which made me extremely discouraged...The company launched a new product, and I had to register the trademark with the Trademark Bureau, so I drafted an official document. Unexpectedly, when the manager saw it, he sneered and said, 'I don't need you to write an essay!' I immediately felt a chill, thinking, 'Isn't this writing an essay?' But I didn't dare to say it out loud...After listening to the manager's words, I flipped through the old drafts and couldn't help but feel discouraged...When I was in school, I got 98 points for writing an invitation to a friend to appreciate chrysanthemums, but now it's not like that at all! Sir, is everything I learned in the past completely useless to me? Were the praises of the teachers in the past all lies? Is it the school's fault, the teacher's fault, or my own fault? Who should be responsible for this mistake? Is there a way to remedy it? I think there must be many people who have the same difficulties as me. Sir, I hope you will be a beacon for our future!" Reply: "Your feet are unrestrained and free, your aspirations are extraordinary, and I am very impressed. The questions you asked can be summarized into two points..."

"What you have learned is not what you are using now." This saying has become a common catchphrase. For example, after becoming an engineering expert, one becomes a professor. This is all because society cannot use it, or even if it can, what he has learned may not be applicable. But your situation cannot be classified into this category. What the school teaches is principles and common sense. It can teach people rules but cannot teach people how to adapt. The things in the world are endless...learn one and infer a hundred. Education has done its best...it depends on the scholar's ability to use what he knows to adapt to things...There is absolutely no rigid article in the world. You are only twenty-one years old and have graduated from high school, so your talent is undoubted. Based on your excellent grades in school, even though you have some difficulties now, you will soon be able to overcome them, so there is no need to be "discouraged." The success of any career must go through some difficulties. The more eager you are to make progress, the greater the difficulties you will encounter, and the more discouraged you will become...This must rely on perseverance to overcome. If you are discouraged by a small setback, you will never be able to achieve great things. You are very confident and have great ambitions, but you were made to "feel a chill" by the manager's laughter. Isn't that cowardly? In the future, there may be things that make you feel a chill from the top of your head to the bottom of your feet, which is our young people's "deeply rooted and intertwined" problems. Moreover, the manager did not laugh coldly and immediately order you to leave, but instead asked you to refer to the old drafts. This is an opportunity to make rapid progress. How can you miss it? Furthermore, the difference in this kind of written text lies in the format, but the reasoning is the same as writing in school...What you have learned in the past is the foundation and cannot be abandoned rashly. If you bravely move forward, the light will not be far away.

Notice: Recently, there have been too many letters from various parties, and the review is more complicated, so the response time may be sooner or later. Letter-writers, please forgive me. In short, this column will answer all letters with complete procedures, but the time will vary.

Body Burned in Millu Road Proven to be a Female Worker from Huzhou 181

▲ Because she had more than forty yuan hidden on her person

▲ Which melted into two silver blocks

The toy sulfur ammunition workshop at No. 4 Ronghua Lane, Fangbang Millu Road, French Concession, caught fire at 0:20 PM the day before yesterday, spreading to neighboring houses and burning a worker to death. The fire brigade pulled out the body and sent it to the Tongren Fuyuan Sub-Hall to wait for an autopsy. The details have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that the deceased was indeed Duan Zhang, a 31-year-old female worker from Huzhou who lived at No. 1 Yongshou Lane, Fangbang Road, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. Her daughter and others knew that the deceased had more than forty yuan hidden on her body. The coroner found two melted silver blocks in front of the deceased's chest, which proved this. Yesterday morning, the patrol room reported to the Second Special District Court, which sent Prosecutor Deng Baosun to the site to verify that the deceased was indeed burned to death before her death. According to the information provided by the foreman, the official ordered that the body be allowed to be claimed by the deceased's son, Duan Zhengming, after signing a guarantee. The deceased had one son and five daughters, all of whom were young. The deceased was a Christian before her death, so the Jesus Church sent personnel to the scene to prepare a coffin and claim the body. The deceased's children will also be taken care of by the church. 1

Important Map Documents Lost 183

▲ Forgotten on a rickshaw in the French Concession

▲ A reward of twenty-five yuan will be given for the return of the original items.

A Russian professor and traveler named Captain N. Diakoff, currently residing at No. 70, Route Cardinal Mercier, French Concession, went to a school on Jing'an Temple Road yesterday afternoon, and then took a rickshaw back to his residence in the French Concession. After getting off the rickshaw, he went straight into his residence and forgot a large leather bag on the rickshaw. Inside was a large map of various regions of China, hundreds of drawings, hundreds of letters of introduction with inscriptions from people in various regions, educational halls, and important government officials, and 200 map orders. These items are the result of Diakoff's decades of travel and painstaking efforts in various parts of China. Once lost, he almost wanted to commit suicide. In addition, there was a passport issued by the Chinese Public Security Bureau, a passport for American Philippine territory, and a passport for French Annam territory. We hope that benevolent people will consider that the above items are of little value to others, but Mr. Diakoff regards them as treasures. Please return the original items to Mr. Diakoff at No. 70, Route Cardinal Mercier, French Concession, and he will reward you with twenty-five yuan.

▲ Family Education Lecture Broadcasting Record: The Great Eastern Bookstore's family education lecture was given yesterday by Mr. Yang Weiyu, deputy director of the China Vocational Education Society, on the topic of "Children's Vocational Cultivation, Part One". He first described the true meaning of the two words "occupation", then described the relationship between children and occupation, and then clarified that whether children are in school or at home, vocational cultivation is necessary. The so-called vocational cultivation and vocational education are completely different. Vocational education is not what children need, but vocational cultivation is necessary for children's education. It is hoped that all families will pay attention to it. ▲ Death of American Insurance Magnate: According to a recent news from the China Life Insurance Promotion Association, Mr. Kingslai, the famous chairman and general manager of the New York Life Insurance Company in the United States, passed away last month. He has served in various important positions in the company for 43 years. Many celebrities from political, business, and academic circles attended the funeral, such as former President Coolidge, Columbia University President Butler, US Army General Harbaugh, New York Times owner Ochs, United Steel Company General Manager Schwab, etc. Although Kingslai grew up in the United States, his ancestor was British, and his father was a frugal small farmer in New England. He was initially educated in local secondary schools, and on holidays he helped his father and relatives cultivate the land. Later, he strived to enter the University of Vermont, providing for his tuition by himself. In 1881, he obtained a bachelor's degree with the highest honors. Afterwards, the university successively awarded him honorary degrees such as Doctor of Laws and Doctor of Philosophy. After Kingslai took charge of the administration of New York Life Insurance Company, the company's internal strength doubled, and the number of life insurance policyholders increased from one million to two and a half million. The company's assets increased from 500 trillion US dollars to 20,000 trillion US dollars. His speeches and papers on life insurance, civic society, and economics, huge works, numbered in the hundreds of thousands of words, not only served as a pioneer in promoting the company's business to flourish, but also made a great contribution to the development of the entire life insurance industry.

▲ China Weekly Advance Suspension of Publication: China Weekly on North Suzhou Road, published for more than a year, has a fair attitude, sharp comments, rich materials, and strong interest. Now, due to internal reorganization, the publication will be suspended one week in advance and will continue to be published as usual on January 7 next year. In order to expand business and reach 10,000 copies this year, all those who subscribe to the newspaper for the whole year before January 10 (the annual subscription fee is three yuan, including postage) will be given a copy of the latest legal compendium compiled by the China Legal Editing Office, which is priced at four yuan. The newspaper's content has also been greatly improved, with the addition of a column on legal knowledge, edited by the editor of the Popular Legal Knowledge Weekly, and plans to publish a January 28 special issue and a series of books. Those who subscribe to the newspaper can purchase it at Dahua, Liming, Huatong and other bookstores on Simaru Road.

Nantong Industrial and Commercial Supplementary School Land Case Submitted to the Ministry of Finance for Verification 193

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education reported that the site of the Nantong County Industrial and Commercial Supplementary School, which was originally owned by the Nantong County Education Bureau-managed supplementary school, was suddenly requested by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance's Sand Field Bureau to be leased to a third party. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education reported this situation to the Ministry of Education, requesting that the Ministry of Finance instruct the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance to cancel the Sand Field Bureau's original document for leasing this school site in order to maintain the school site and benefit the progress of education. The Ministry of Education has submitted this situation to the Ministry of Finance for verification and instruction to proceed.

20th Anniversary Celebration of Nantong Central Experimental Primary School 194

The Jiangsu Provincial Nantong Central Experimental Primary School held its 20th anniversary celebration on the 11th and 12th of this month. The alumni association also held an achievement exhibition and a parents' meeting, and invited celebrities to give speeches, such as Wu Zhihui, Wu Yan Yin, etc. Everyone had words of support. The school's achievements were divided into eighteen rooms. On the morning of the 11th, at 10:00 AM, a commemorative ceremony was held. After the principal's keynote report, speeches were given by guests, family members, and alumni. In the afternoon, the alumni association held a meeting. After the chairman's report, alumni gave successive speeches and discussed association affairs, and elected staff before the meeting adjourned. In the evening, a variety show and film screening were held.

Junior High School Curriculum Standards (5)

English 1. Objectives 195

(1) Practice using simple English relevant to daily life.

(2) Establish a good foundation for advanced English studies.

(3) Enable students to develop their language experience from the English perspective.

(4) Enable students to increase their interest in studying foreign affairs from the English perspective.

2. Time Allocation 196

(1) Five hours per week.

(2) The weekly time should not be divided into specific hours dedicated to textbooks or grammar, etc.

3. Curriculum Outline 197

(1) First Academic Year

㈠ Various fixed-pattern short sentence groups, mostly those that can be illustrated with real objects, diagrams, or actions, such as command groups and performance groups (aural and oral practice, reading all translated editions and all commonly spelled printed and handwritten versions 丨丨 handwritten versions include old-style continuous handwriting and new-style handwritten printing, copying and dictating commonly spelled words 丨丨 handwritten printing is the general principle, replacing sentence construction). ㈡ Various non-fixed-pattern short sentence groups, such as practical conversations on specific topics, short stories, small plays, etc. 丨丨丨 gradually increasing from the first semester (same as item one). ㈢ Short classroom terms (same as item one). ㈣ Phonemes and combinations extracted from the materials in items one, two, and three (aural and oral practice). ㈤ General understanding and application of pronunciation parts, methods, and sound category differentiation. ㈥ Phonetic symbols corresponding to the materials in item four 丨丨 International Phonetic Alphabet is the general principle (identification, listening, pointing out, reading). ㈦ Upper and lowercase letters of printed and old-style handwritten fonts (identification). ㈧ Upper and lowercase letters of the new-style handwritten printing font (identification of shapes, understanding of structures, tracing, independent writing). ㈨ Posture, pen holding, hand movement, etc. for writing (understanding, application). ㈩ Grammatical points that must be pointed out in the materials in items one, two, and three 丨丨 including differentiation and changes in parts of speech and sentence patterns (understanding, application). (Note) Grammar is the old name for grammar. ㈩㈠ Various corresponding temporary teaching materials (usage is carefully considered according to special learning motivations). ㈩㈡ Information on the lifestyles of foreign people, etc. 丨丨 especially those of English-speaking nations 丨丨 should be pointed out in various teaching materials (understanding).

(2) Second Academic Year

㈠ Same as item two in the first academic year (except for partial oral editions and partial textbook editions, the rest is the same). ㈡ Short sentences extracted from the first teaching material (item four in item one). ㈢ The third item of the civil first year (same as item one). ㈣ Brief passages that have been close to and not lightened to oral practice in the first, second, and third items of teaching (reading and meaning if there are no new words in the printed book or if there are new words but no more than two or three percent, oral or fetching words). ㈤ Usage of the angles (understanding the application). ㈥ Reading, copying, imitating, and filling out extremely simple and fixed-pattern usual documents and the like (printed or handwritten). ㈦ Grammatical points that must be pointed out in the first, second, third, fourth, and sixth items of teaching materials 丨丨 including the differentiation and changes in parts of speech and name styles (understanding and application). ㈧ Same as item eleven in the first academic year. ㈨ Item twelve of the first academic year.

(3) Third Academic Year

㈠ Same as item one in the second academic year (oral or manual imitation, the rest is the same). ㈡ Same as item two in the second academic year. ㈢ Same as item three in the first year. ㈣ Short, simple narrative language, descriptive language, language, and argumentative language (item one). ㈤ Brief passages of printed matter in which new words from four or five percent to six or seven percent of the materials are close to and have not previously been aurally and orally practiced in the first, second, third, and fourth items. Same as item four in the second academic year, plus the practice of verbally or manually supplementing the remaining meanings. ㈥ Simple and fixed-pattern usual letters and documents (same as item six in the second year). ㈦ Grammatical points that must be pointed out in the above six items of teaching materials 丨丨 Sentence classification and the differentiation and changes of sentence patterns (understanding the application). ㈧ Same as item eleven in the first school year. ㈨ Same as item twelve in the first school year. (Note) The total number of words in the teaching materials for the above three academic years is approximately 3,000 words, of which 2,000 words must be used in Thoundide's Teaching Word Hood Middle, which is commonly used in 2,000 words, and the remaining 1,000 words do not necessarily have to be taken from the third thousand words in the book.

4. Outline of Implementation Methods 198

(1) Important Operating Items

㈠ Listening practice: 1. Listen to the sound and understand the meaning, 2. Listen to the sound and distinguish the sound. ㈡ Speaking practice: 1. Speaking alone 2. Oral questions 3. Verbal imitation of sentences. ㈢ Eye viewing practice: 1. Identify the font, 2. Silent reading. ㈣ Handwriting practice: 1. Write the font alone 2. Dictate and memorize words and sentences 3. Manually imitate sentences ㈤ Listening and speaking practice: 1. Oral imitation 2. Oral answer ㈥ Listening and eye viewing practice: 1. Look at the phonetic symbols or spelling while listening ㈦ Listening and handwriting practice: 1. Dictate silently while listening ㈧ Practice of seeing and speaking: 1. Reading aloud ㈨ Practice of seeing and writing: 1. Copying fonts 12. Copying words and sentences. ㈩ Practice of seeing, hearing, and speaking: 1. Imitating the sound while looking at the phonetic symbols or spelling

(2) Key Teaching Points

㈠ Stagger the start of listening, speaking, reading, and writing exercises, with listening and speaking as the first phase, reading as the second phase, and writing as the third phase. Roughly, it is only at the end of the first phase that the practice of the four types of work can be achieved. Work in one phase should be practiced until there is a slight grasp before moving to the next phase, so as to avoid many new difficulties gathering at the same time and making it difficult to break free.

㈡ In the first year, special emphasis is placed on listening and speaking to make the preliminary work solid and to enable students to develop an appropriate attitude towards foreign language learning. In the second year, equal emphasis is placed on listening, speaking, reading, and writing, so that students can develop evenly in all aspects. In the third year, special emphasis is placed on reading to make it suitable for the most common uses of general students.

㈢ Explain all tasks with a clear method first, so that students can accurately understand the real needs and have a corresponding learning motivation. ㈣ All exercises should start from the whole sentence or return to the whole sentence, so that students can use complete sentences of language and writing.

㈤ Pay attention to repeated practice to make it pure and familiar.

㈥ Fully review old lessons to make them permanently remembered.

㈦ Within the scope of the material that students have already learned, encourage free application so that what is learned can be related to life.

㈧ Group practice and individualized learning complement each other, so that it can be popular and suitable for individuality.

㈨ Use English as much as possible and Chinese as little as possible, so that students can get more opportunities to practice and learn more pure English.

㈩ Always give instructions on learning methods to increase learning efficiency.

㈩㈠ Examine whether the students' work is correct from time to time, and make every effort to prevent errors. Once an error is found, it should be quickly and thoroughly corrected to avoid avoidable errors, and unavoidable errors should not become habits. ㈩㈡ Use special practice and explanations to prevent or correct the most common errors of all students, so that the greatest difficulties of the whole body can be economically relieved.

㈩㈢ Always pay attention to the students' achievements so that the progress can be adjusted according to the pre-determined plan.

㈩㈣ Always make students aware of their progress so that they can stimulate interest and be brave to learn.

㈩㈤ Before the new material is practiced in speaking, there must be listening practice first, so that there is adequate preparation and errors can be reduced.

㈩㈥ The meaning of new materials, except for those that cannot be explained in Chinese, should be expressed by other means so that students can learn more pure English and reach the point of thinking in English as early as possible.

㈩㈦ Except for those who read without oral practice, the new material should generally be practiced in advance during teaching time so that students can continue to study on their own to avoid errors.

㈩㈧ In addition to reviewing the original organization of the old materials separately, they must also be mixed and reorganized separately in order to review and enable communication, connection, change, and active use.

㈩㈨ Use games, competitions, and tableau forms to review old materials to increase interest and practice application.

㈡㈩ Oral practice should not only focus on the correctness of each part but also on the fluency of the whole part to make it consistent with the nature of the language.

㈡㈠ Phoneme analysis should generally start from the materials that have already been practiced orally and orally, so that it is practical and can be effective.

㈡㈡ Phoneme practice should be analyzed only to the smallest practical unit to avoid too much analysis, which is not practical and wastes effort.

㈡㈢ In the practice of listening and pronouncing sounds, make full use of the aids in speech, such as the recognition and reading of phonetic symbols, the observation of pronunciation positions, etc., to make it easier for students to grasp.

㈡㈣ Pay attention to the comprehensive changes in the phonemes that should be in words and sentences, such as assimilation, connection, etc., to make them fit the situation of living language.

㈡㈤ The sequence of work should be from reading aloud to so that it can be

use and is easier to increase the speed of reading.

㈡㈥ For reading that has been practiced orally in advance, pay attention to the understanding of the general meaning and not to the unimportant new words, so that reading can meet the needs of life.

㈡㈦ The correctness of the shape and the speed of writing should be precise and practical.

Functional work, so that it can be practical.

㈡㈧ Grammatical points should be pointed out from the materials that have already been mastered, and they should be collected, connected, and organized in a systematic way, so that they are practical everywhere and can clarify the general outline of English.

㈡㈨ The grammatical points should be pointed out from the familiar materials, and supplementary practice should be added as needed so that they can not only be understood but also be easily applied.

㈢㈩ Grammatical teaching should pay special attention to the differences between English and language in order to easily learn more pure English and to perceive the structural characteristics of the two languages.

㈢㈠ All oral and manual creations must be strictly limited to the scope and strive to create freely at will, so that more pure English can be learned.

Kunshan Fish Farm Attached to the Fisheries School 201

The Wusong Fisheries School, in order to practically test fish farming techniques, has an attached fish farm in Kunshan. Since the January 28th Incident, the farm's finances have been severely strained, but it has striven to maintain operations without faltering. Recently, observing that the fish farming methods of the local villagers were conservative and invariably led to failure, the school, in addition to compiling and printing "A Simple Explanation of Fish Farming" research reports for distribution and publicity, has established a guidance center to answer inquiries from all sectors. Since its establishment, numerous letters requesting guidance have been received from nearby land reclamation companies, the Kunshan County Education Bureau, the Zhejiang Provincial Experimental Farm, and the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau, among others.

Results of Qinghua Middle School Speech Contest 203

Qinghua Elementary and Middle School in Paomapu Zhangjiabang was founded six years ago by the famous lawyer Zhang Shuhua. The school’s performance has been improving daily. This semester, the student body has reached 350. Yesterday at 2 PM, the school held a Mandarin speech contest, presided over by Principal Zhang Shuhua. Liu Haisu, president of the Shanghai Art College; Cui Jianwu, president of the Daodong Girls' School; and Guo Chunqing, president of the Yiyi Girls' School were invited as judges. Nine middle school students and twelve elementary school students participated in the speeches. As a result, the third grade of junior high school and the fifth grade of elementary school won the grade-level championship. The individual winners were Ouyang Shu, first place in the middle school group; Tang Renjiang, second place; and Zhang Qianyi, third place. In the elementary school group, Liu Yunrang won first place, Fan Ruoying won second place, and Lin Peiji won third place. Each winner was awarded a championship mirror plaque on the spot.

Jiangsu-Zhejiang Private Middle School Basketball and Soccer Tournament

John's University Middle School Wins Basketball Championship Runner-Up; Shanghai University Loses to John's 19-32; Defeats Jinling 40-28; John's Also Soccer Runner-Up, Defeating Huilan 6-0 205

The Jiangsu-Zhejiang Private Middle School Athletic Association's basketball and soccer tournament, which began last Friday at St. John's University in Fanwangdu in this city, concluded yesterday. The soccer championship was won by Jinling Middle School on Monday. The basketball championship and runner-up, as well as the soccer runner-up, were all decided yesterday, as expected. John's University Middle School won the basketball championship, with Shanghai University Middle School as the runner-up. John's University Middle School also won the soccer runner-up. The details of yesterday's matches are as follows:

John's University Wins Basketball Championship 206

▲Defeats Shanghai University Middle School 32-19

John's and Shanghai University Middle School, which won the right to compete for the basketball championship, faced off in the St. John's recreation room yesterday morning. Both teams had respectable talent. Shanghai University was tall overall, while John's was short and nimble. In terms of skill, John's had better coordination and quicker movements. John's launched a steady attack, and the momentum was favorable. Shanghai University followed closely behind, maintaining control but without a chance to surpass. In the first half, John's led 16-8, with a four-goal lead. Starting in the second half, Shanghai University took the offensive and seized the initiative. For a moment, their momentum was overwhelming, and they suddenly exceeded the score, taking an 18-16 lead over John's. In this tense atmosphere, John's intensified its efforts and slowly progressed. The "Little Five Warriors" each showed their drive, with each point breaking through. Everyone raced to claim credit. On the scoreboard, the score was reversed and exceeded. From then on, Shanghai University was once again at a disadvantage and struggled to break free, without building any momentum. John's had smooth sailing and won 32-19, winning the championship. The scores are as follows:

Shanghai United Middle School Football Final Between Pudong and Shanghai University Postponed to the 23rd of This Month 221

The Shanghai Middle School Sports Federation’s annual football competition, which began several weeks ago, has been going on for several weeks. The teams that have won the right to compete in the finals are Shanghai University High School in the Upper Group and Pudong Middle School in the Sea Group. According to the schedule, the two sides were scheduled to hold the final today afternoon. However, since the Shanghai University High School has been participating in the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Sports Federation of China organized by the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Province, in reality it is difficult to divide time. Therefore, it requested the Middle School Football Committee to reschedule the final scheduled for today. The Football Committee believes that the Shanghai University request is not without reason, so it has agreed with Pudong Middle School and decided to change the date to Friday afternoon (December 23rd) at 3 PM at the China Football Field. Financial and Gold Market Surge 228

(Soaring by 8.4 Taels) Yesterday's market continued to reach a peak, with a firm and buoyant state. The difference between the morning and afternoon markets was only four to five taels. Ultimately, it surged by 8.4 taels. The initial rise was mainly due to the continued decline in the silver market. Although exchange rates and American cotton rose, they did not have a significant impact. Later, due to the tense trend in foreign exchange, buyers on the floor were active, and the market improved further. The fluctuations in between were only around two taels. The afternoon market was particularly sharp, already exceeding the 810 tael mark. The Central Bank opened and injected 105 bars of spot gold in the morning at a price of 807 taels and 5 qian, which was sold by Tong Feng Heng. Furthermore, the short seller Heng Xing bought more than 100 bars of December gold from the long sellers Qian Chang Xiang, etc., with a discount of 4 qian, which was lower than last week, because the spot inventory seemed to be increasing.

(Morning Market Showing Promise) From the early opening of the January contract, it immediately rose by 1.6 qian, to 803 taels and 2 qian, followed by fluctuations of four to five qian, reaching 803 taels. Because Hua Bi absorbed 6,875 pounds of January English gold, and the Japanese bank bought 25 US dollars for March, and Yuan Xing Yong, Nei Xing, Da Xing Yong, etc. bought in, it immediately added more than 2 taels, to 805 taels and 7 qian. Fu Yu, Tian Feng, Yong Yuan Mao, Yong Yuan Tai, and some speculators sold off, and the March US $25 could be done at 28 yuan for December, so the price fell back more than 1 tael, to 804 taels. Soon, Heng Yu, He Yuan Tai, Hong Kang Yong, and zero-lot buyers competed to buy. Both the HSBC listed exchange rates for English and American currencies shrank by 125, and Mitsui absorbed 125 US dollars for March, and 28 yuan could be sold for December, so at 9:30 it was 807 taels. In the blink of an eye, the exchange rates of English and American currencies shrank again by 125. Unfortunately, the price of gold did not improve, because the previous market was already done by people. At this time, it stood at more than 806 taels. Then, Feng, Yong Fu Tai, Tian Feng, Yong Zhao Feng Chang, etc. sold some, and HSBC, etc. sold 125 US dollars for February to Mitsui, and the price of gold fell by more than 1 tael, until 10:30 it was 805 taels and 1 qian. Hu Chang, Yuan Heng, Fu Yu, Fu Tai, Heng Yuan Tai, Yuan Mao Yong, etc. came to buy, and Hua Bi absorbed 28 yuan for January, and Mitsui absorbed 1,875 for March, so it rose again by 3 taels. At 11:00 it was 808 taels. After entering, Qian Chang Xiang, Yuan Ji Yong, and retail long positions took the opportunity to sell, sharply falling by 2 taels. At 11:30 it was 806 taels and 2 qian. Suddenly, Tong Feng Heng sold 105 bars of spot gold to the Central Bank, causing the price to rise by more than 1 tael, and Yi Feng and Da De Cheng, etc. followed up. At 11:50 it was 807 taels and 8 qian. The noon closing was 807 taels and 4 qian.

(Soaring to 812 Taels After the Closing) The afternoon market opened at 808 taels. Later, because Zhi Feng Yong, Wan Xing Shun Li, etc. sold out, it fell back to 807 taels. Mai Hang offered 1,875 US dollars for March. Then Hua Bi absorbed 9,375 for December, and January was settled at the same price. Furthermore, Bing Xing, Heng Xing, Da Xing Yong, Da De Cheng, etc. had a strong buying intention, and Fu Yu was particularly determined to drag in. The market situation became more and more sharp, rising by 4 taels, and there were few positions left. At 2:45 it was 811 taels. Then Zhao Feng Chang, Feng Yong Shun Li, Yong Feng Heng Yu, etc. took this opportunity to sell, but US dollars were settled very actively, and banks were still willing to buy, so the price of gold could not rise any further, but fell by 2.5 taels. At 4:00 it was 808 taels and 5 qian. Afterwards, it seemed to be looking up. Heng Xing bought in on behalf of a certain bank, and Hong Xing, Sen Chang Yong, and Wu Pin, etc. bought in, causing the price to rise back by 1.5 taels. From 4:00 to 4:30 the fluctuations were only a few qian. Then it closed at 810 taels, up 8.4 taels compared to the previous day. After the closing, it suddenly rose again by 2 taels, reaching 812 taels. However, buyers were not happy. The downstream price was about 811 taels. According to the full day, the highest price was 811 taels, and the lowest price was 803 taels, a difference of 8 taels. The discount for bare gold decreased because the supply was constant, adding only 10 taels and 5 qian. The initial listed price for US dollars decreased by 125, so it was calculated as 861 taels with a discount of 54.5 taels. Soon it was changed to a reduction of 125 and also changed to 865 taels, with a discount of 60 taels to 57.8 taels. In the afternoon, it was 57 taels to 58 taels, and then 54.5 taels. Compared with the previous day, there was no significant difference. The charge was 800 taels to 807 taels, the additional charge was 807 taels, and 810 taels in the afternoon.

American Cotton Firm, British Cotton Flat and Weak 242

Yesterday, American cotton initially became firm from calm due to bad weather and a lack of sellers. Later, due to the settlement of some long positions, it reacted and weakened. The price of prompt goods rose by 5 to 9 pounds. The price of spot goods rose by 5 pounds. British cotton futures fell by 2 points, and spot goods rose by 3 points. Egyptian cotton spot goods rose by 11 points. Indian cotton market was closed. The original telegram is on the left (telegram on the 12th).
