Yarn Exchange New Year Holiday Announcement 243

▲Closed for Four Days▲

The Yarn Cloth Exchange has decided on the duration of the New Year holiday. The cotton business will be conducted until the 27th of this month, and the cotton yarn will be conducted until the 29th. The 30th will be for handling delivery procedures. From December 31, 1932, to January 3, 1933, the market will be closed in accordance with the regulations. The market will reopen as usual on January 4.

Grain Prices Most Fiercely Rise in January 244

▲Dalian Gang Collects, Floating Long Positions Rush In▲

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices of each month were generally stable. Since the price of foreign wheat fell by about 1 to 2 jiao, the market sentiment was still flat at the beginning. However, as various factories entered the market and outside merchants continued to buy, and merchants from Dong Province also slightly increased their purchases, the market sentiment gradually became firmer. When the market opened in the afternoon, the prices of each month rose again in unison, especially the rise in January was even more frantic. Since there was some short covering in this month and the market sentiment was already tight, the Dalian Gang tried their best to buy, and general floating long positions also joined in to rush in. Therefore, the price rose step by step with a very strong momentum. In particular, it was also rumored that Fuxin did not have much raw materials and would stop production, which made the market sentiment even better. However, Fufeng had some sellers in January, and Fuxin also slightly sold in the forward term, but the amount was small. The subsequent trend will depend on whether the Dalian Gang will continue to move and then determine the rise and fall. As a result, this month rose by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day, January rose by 4 fen, February and March rose by 1.5 fen, April rose by 1.75 fen, and May rose by 2 fen.

Wheat Futures Continue to be Stable and Buoyant 245

丨Few Chips, Transactions Still Sparse丨

Yesterday, the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon still showed signs of stability and buoyancy for each month. Although the price of foreign wheat was slightly lower by 1 to 2 jiao, the exchange rate shrank again, which inevitably affected the pricing of wheat. This kind of imagination was entirely based on temporary emotional considerations. Since the foreign wheat already ordered by the factories in this port is sufficient for use until the new wheat next year, they are slightly panicked because they cannot continue to receive it. Moreover, due to the re-buoyancy of the flour market, the market sentiment is inevitably rising, but transactions are still sparse, mainly because the chips are not abundant. As a result, February rose by 4 fen compared to the previous day, March rose by 3 fen, April rose by 2 fen, and there were no other changes.

Chicago Wheat Uneven 246

Chicago wheat on Monday the 12th fell due to poor export demand and selling by the East. The volume traded on the 10th was 20 million bushels. The prices on the 12th are listed below. The closing price was lower than the previous day: December contract 4.500 Down 0.375 May contract 48.875 Down 0.375 July contract 49.100 Up 0.125

Customer Xian (Type of Rice) Devalued and Sold 247

Yesterday, the arrival of customer xian became increasingly popular, but the market inventory was already around 40,000 bags. Firms were afraid of affecting the market and did not release samples or announce the arrival volume, so the arrival number was unknown. However, some lenders, in view of the arrival of many river rice boats and the decline in prices after the sale became sluggish, and a large amount of foreign wheat existed, were more willing to devalue and sell in order to seek economic circulation. Except for the Xiang machine red rice, which was in short supply and actively sold, allowing the market to support, other rice depreciated slightly by 1 jiao. The price decline slightly caused inquiries from various Min province groups. The Northern gang also tried to handle hundreds of bags, mostly for the Min province capital gangs. It was reported that 827 bags of Jiangxi machine late rice were priced at 8 yuan, and 142 bags of machine early rice were priced at 7 yuan 8 jiao half. 1,500 bags of Hunan machine red rice were priced at 8 yuan 7 yuan 9 jiao 7 fen to 7 yuan 9 jiao. Also, 380 bags of red rice were priced at 6 yuan half. 900 bags of Wuhu machine yuan were priced at 9 yuan to 8 yuan 7 or 8 jiao. 384 bags of Anqing yuan were priced at 8 yuan to 7 yuan 9 jiao.

Miscellaneous Grains

Lively Transactions of Raw Peanuts Last Week 248

丨East and West Ocean Companies Absorbed at Production Areas at Bottom Prices丨

Last week, the market for raw peanuts saw lively inflows and outflows again. However, the quality of the goods varied, so the prices varied. High-quality goods generally rose. The total transactions for the week were over 4,340 bags and 280 tons, including 1 lot of Cheng raw peanuts at 6 taels 45 qian. The goods were relatively inferior. On Tuesday, another 200 bags were opened at 6 taels 9 qian to 7 qian 8 fen. 200 tons of Qufu raw peanuts were priced at 6 taels 8 qian. Eight centralized Guang raw peanuts were priced at 6 taels 4 qian half. Liji raw peanuts were priced at 6 taels 3 qian half to 3 qian, totaling 300 bags. On Wednesday, 200 bags each of Tancheng Taolin raw peanuts were opened, priced at 6 taels 9 qian to 7 taels. 40 tons of Xuzhou raw peanuts were opened, priced at 6 taels 3 qian. On Thursday, a total of 2,000 bags were opened, including Tancheng raw peanuts at 7 taels, Xuzhou raw peanuts at 6 taels 3 qian, Kaifeng raw peanuts at 6 taels 7 qian to 6 qian, Zhongxing raw peanuts at 6 taels 9 qian, and eight centralized Guang raw peanuts at 6 taels 5 qian half. On Friday and Saturday, a total of 1,200 bags were opened, Tancheng raw peanuts at 7 taels to 7 taels 2 qian, Liji raw peanuts at 6 taels 7 qian. At the weekend, 40 tons of Kaifeng raw peanuts were opened, priced at 6 taels 8 qian half. 40 bags of Zhongxing raw peanuts were priced at 7 taels.

Qingdao Newsletter. Hulled peanuts are being absorbed by East and West Ocean companies at the local level. Because high-quality goods are scarce, they are turning to ordinary goods. The previous market price was 6 yuan 7 or 8 jiao, and the current release price is 7 yuan 1 jiao, which is being heavily purchased. The next grade is 7 yuan, and the next grade is 6 yuan 6 or 7 jiao, and the lowest grade is 6 yuan 4 or 5 jiao.

Sugar Market: Newly Arrived Zhangzhou Brown Sugar Expected in Shanghai Soon 249

Yesterday's overseas sugar market reports indicated no changes in New York spot prices. Futures for December, May, and September also remained unchanged. Only the futures for January, March, and July saw a slight increase of about one pound. London futures for December and May both decreased slightly by one pence and seventeen and a half points, while March decreased by one pence and ten points. Java white sugar also remained unchanged. Locally, Shanghai's sugar market saw the benchmark price rise further to over 800 taels, and the momentum tightened again. In the morning, Changxing Trading Company offered 1,000 bags of No. 24 coarse granulated white sugar at a price of 15 taels and 4 mace, already showing signs of an increase. In the afternoon, the guild's trading session maintained a positive atmosphere, with more buying than selling, pushing prices up another 2.5 fen to 15 taels, 4 mace, and 2.5 fen. Later in the session, prices reached 15 taels and 4 mace and 5 fen, an improvement of 6.25 li compared to the day before. No. 20 medium granulated white sugar was traded in small lots at 14 taels and 7 mace to 7 mace and 5 fen. No. 18 medium granulated white sugar remained stable at 14 taels and 4 mace. Numbers 8, 9, and 10 red sugar remained as stable as before. As for locally produced ice crystal brown sugar, Zhenxin Factory offered several hundred bags at a price of 11 taels and 1 mace. Additionally, Dalai Company offered several dozen pieces of Bagua brand brown sugar at a price of 10 taels and 6 qian, which was still being bought. Gaozhuang Jian ice was also offered in several dozen boxes at a price of 10 taels and 7 mace and 3 li per unit. According to news from Xiamen, this year's harvest of Zhangzhou brown sugar produced in Zhangzhou is abundant and is already being brought to market. Therefore, price inquiries are frequently received via telegrams and letters. It is expected that shipments will arrive in Shanghai within the next few days.

North-South Goods: Longkou Vermicelli Sales to Surge, Prices Already Rebounding 250

Longkou vermicelli supply has recently surged, with customer bids once reaching as low as 18 taels. In recent days, prices have gradually improved, and yesterday's opening price tightened further, rising to 18.5 taels. Most of the goods have already been purchased by various firms, and with the winter sales season approaching, demand is expected to be strong, so the firms have been raising their asking prices, and there is a potential for further price increases. According to telegrams from the production area, the price per package is 24 taels and 9 qian, and the market is expected to rise further.

Silk and Tea: Raw Silk Sales Strong, Especially to the US 251

Raw silk sales have shown renewed vigor. American silk factories have a strong demand for goods, as they are currently weaving spring silk. Therefore, the price of American silk has been increasing daily. Due to the continuous strong sales in recent days, Chinese merchants are holding onto their silk stocks, waiting for better prices before selling, resulting in price increases of around 50 taels in the past ten days. Most transactions involve standard silk. French silk only accounts for a hundred or so pieces of Sichuan silk.

Oil Market: Xiutong Oil Customer Bids Announced 252

Since the order regarding Xiutong oil, existing stocks have been sold out, and there have been no transactions for a long time. Recently, however, several hundred barrels of Wan Yu, Dayou Heng, and other brands have arrived, and the customer has come to Shanghai to discuss opening customer bids with local firms. Bids were announced the day before yesterday, with prices for Wan Yu and Dayou Heng set at 23 taels and 4 qian, and prices for Xia Taiheng and Jifeng Heng set at 22 taels and 6 qian. These are all customer bids, totaling a thousand pieces, which have been distributed to various oil and sesame firms. Inland firms, upon hearing the news, have rushed to purchase, fearing that the limited quantity will leave them empty-handed.

Piece Goods: Shortage of Material for Jodhpur Pants and Greatcoats 253

丨Jodhpur Cloth and Real Horse Lining丨

"Jodhpur cloth" is currently experiencing an extreme shortage, with sales surging, supplies interrupted, and market inventories greatly depleted. Prices are increasing steadily. Yesterday, a 1005 quality cloth was being hoarded by sellers, asking for 67 taels. Tailors selling remnants were asking for 10 yuan and 5 jiao per yard. "Real horse lining" is also extremely scarce, with prices up several points from last week. Yesterday, first-grade real horse sleeve lining was sold wholesale for 1 tael and 4 qian, and second-grade goods were sold for 1 tael, 3 qian, and 2.5 fen net.

Hardware: Hardware Prices Trending Upward 254

Although the Shanghai hardware market has not seen significant progress in sales recently, the arrival of goods has been extremely limited, and existing inventories are low. As a result, hardware prices have been rising across the board. Items such as tinplate, plain white iron, square steel, triangular iron, chopped foreign silver dollars, new lead wire, white lead sheet, new pan yuan, and cut iron are all reportedly increasing in price. Other items that have been quiet for a long time, such as blue lead and solder, are also showing signs of rapid price increases. In general, prices are soaring, and supplies are scarce, so the market price is unlikely to decrease in the short term.

Overseas telegrams: Yesterday's Reuters report indicated that English tinplate prices increased by 2 shillings, with 90-pound plates at 17 shillings and 2 pence, and 100-pound plates at 18 shillings. Double-linked 90-pound plates were at 35 shillings, and 100-pound plates were at 36 shillings and 6 pence. American prices increased by 2.5 jiao, with 90-pound plates at 4 yuan, and 100-pound plates at 4 yuan and 2.5 jiao. However, there are still inquiries and negotiations for English goods in Shanghai. American goods are seeing little interest due to the high US exchange rate. In addition, there have been few changes in other markets, so local firms have not been placing orders.

Another telegram from London indicated that tin, lead, and solder prices all fell. The decline in tin prices is due to the failure of the New York conference. Zinc prices remained unchanged.

Free Talk

A Love Letter Without a Price 278

— Qi Bian

Yu Mei:

Another night has passed, it is now the morning of October 11th. Every night is the same, my hands tightly embrace you, embrace you and kiss you, smile at you, I completely forget that you are not by my side, embracing only my own hard bones, my emaciated body...

Yu Mei, I have nothing to say, I have said everything to you, the emotions of these past few days are indescribable, my depression deepens day by day, my previous patience, I can no longer endure now, my cry, I am sighing, I stomp my feet, sometimes I am simply so angry that I want to destroy myself immediately, destroy all women, destroy this entire world!

I truly never imagined that I am so pitiful, seeing only pairs of lovers walking hand in hand, pairs of sweet-talking lovebirds, why don't I have this kind of happiness? What a joke, I am stronger than all of them in everything, this is a fact, I especially understand women's psychology, understand the true meaning of love, and am so dedicated to love, so responsible, why don't I have a lover? No! Why isn't my lover by my side? Heavens! Is this my destiny? Is there something playing tricks on me, deliberately making me suffer for a few more years before I can find happiness? Yu, everything is in your hands, you will eventually be mine, why deliberately "come so late"! Do you know? Youth cannot be regained, although our spirit will always be youthful, our hearts will always be innocent and tender like children, our love will always burn like a volcano, but time is precious after all! Alas! Why do we have to be separated by the ends of the earth? Why do you want to give me hardship and trap yourself in loneliness?

Yu Mei, I can't bear to tell you about my life these past few days, indeed, I am destroying myself, all day and all night I am immersed in Fenjiu wine, every time I come back from outside drunk, my mind is so confused that I don't know anything, only your shadow is still in front of me, I hold onto the stairs, thinking it is your white lotus-like arms, I hold onto them tightly, I lower my head to kiss them, but, alas! They are just stairs after all, they are a piece of lifeless wood!

Falling onto the bed, I didn't take off my shoes or clothes, and naturally didn't cover myself with the blanket before going to sleep, this sleep will last until the next morning. Yu Mei, you are smart, you completely understand, right? Why do I drink so desperately? In order to avoid insomnia, in order to avoid being unable to get through the long nights of longing, in order to avoid facing your photos and causing me to suffer so much that I want to die... Alas! My beloved Yu, can you bear to see your Heng brother wasting himself like this? His body is your body, his health is your health!

I really can't bear to ruin my body, and I'm not just complaining because of lost love, deliberately drinking, I really can't suppress my heart that misses you, I am sleepless and tearful every night because of thinking of you!

Alas! Yu Mei, what can I say? Everything is the evil created by the economy, everything is the pain created by the economy, what can I say?…

You are too cruel! I truly never imagined that you would treat me this way. Why don't you give me even one letter? If I could just see a sweet letter from you every day, I would definitely get a lot of comfort and would never waste my body like this, sinking into an irredeemable sea of ​​bitterness. Ping, why haven't you sent a letter? Could something unexpected have happened?

·······

Your slave Heng, who loves you deeply and belongs to you forever.

Yu Mei's Reply

Mr. Heng: Please spend less time, I simply can't understand this kind of letter! Li Yu

"Stupid" and "Smart" 279

— Zi Xia

Regarding the many amazing inventions in European and American countries, friends often have this kind of feeling; alas, Westerners are so smart! This means admiring the intelligence of Westerners and feeling ashamed of Chinese people's inferiority. In fact, what about Chinese people? Those who say Chinese people are stupid are the truly stupid ones.

According to the views of smart people, everything should be "sitting back and enjoying the fruits of labor." For example, the ox works hard to plow the fields, and when the crops grow, the horse leisurely goes to eat them. How stupid the ox is, and how smart the horse is. Chinese people are like this, unwilling to be a hardworking, stupid ox.

Don't believe it? You just take the formula of "ox" and "horse" to extrapolate. For example, if someone invents an electric light, we can use it to play cards. If someone invents a steam engine, we can use it to travel. If someone invents an airplane, we can use it to fuel internal wars. If someone invents the radio, we can lie on the sofa and listen leisurely. We can even use the invention of 606 to more boldly engage in the "romantic affairs" of "talented scholars." People bury themselves in the laboratory, exhausting their life's energy, even the painstaking research and continuous experiments of their sons and grandsons. When the experiment succeeds, we can safely "sit back and enjoy the fruits of labor." You think this is so cost-effective; therefore, Chinese people are not stupid, Chinese people are truly smart.

If Newton were a Chinese person, I think when he saw that ripe and red apple falling from the tree, he would definitely not hesitate to quickly pick it up and take a few bites. What he would think is "this apple tastes pretty good," or "it would be best if one or two more fell down," and would never think "why doesn't this apple fly upwards?" Even more, he would never bury himself in research because of this stupid question. Fortunately, Newton was a foreigner, so this fool finally discovered the three laws of universal gravitation because of this apple.

Among our ancestors, it is said that there was also a great fool called Yu Gong. Although the big mountain that hindered the road was finally moved away by him and his sons and grandsons, the sneer of the clever man Zhisou can still be faintly heard to this day. This smile broke off the foolishness of the Chinese people, so Chinese people have become smart people for generations.

However, smart people, remember, smart people can sometimes be misled by their own cleverness!

The Eiffel Tower in Paris 280

— Zhi Sheng

Towering into the clouds, the Eiffel Tower standing tall on the banks of the Seine in Paris is one of the greatest buildings in the world. This tower is a memorial to the "Centenary of the French Republic". Its magnificent and solemn architecture is intended to inspire citizens and tourists to admire it, thereby arousing personal striving and self-encouragement. At the same time, this tower is also closely related to the beauty of Paris.

The tower is 300 meters high, rectangular in shape, and entirely framed with steel bars. The base of the tower is divided into four legs, occupying a very large area. From bottom to top, it gradually shrinks, divided into three layers. The lowest layer has restaurants, coffee shops, newspaper stands, and other facilities to meet the temporary needs of tourists. The top layer has been opened as a radio station, and tourists are now unable to climb to the very top.

To climb the Eiffel Tower, you have to take the elevator up from the door opened under the tower on the right side of the front. At the same time, a spiral staircase is built in the tower, which can be walked around and up.

Whenever the sun is shining and the wind is mild, climbing to the extreme end of the tower is like being in the sky. From here, overlooking Paris is truly shocking. The vast Paris city can be seen at a glance, the Seine River meandering like a white silk, the nearby streets small to the point of being indescribable, and the vehicles and pedestrians coming and going are only like tiny animals wriggling around. At dusk, the lights of Paris are like tens of thousands of stars, and the Seine River, which runs through the center of Paris, is even more extraordinarily white, and the beauty of the scenery is truly unparalleled.

But this Eiffel Tower, which can strongly stimulate people's senses, has become an advertising tower for the Citroen car factory in the dark night. Around the tower, various colors of electric lights are used, from the top to the lowest layer, to continuously connect and form the seven letters of Citroen, appearing and disappearing from time to time, even one or twenty kilometers away from Paris, it can be seen very clearly. The building famous in the history of art has now been completely commercialized.

××××

My Ideal Lover 281

— Jian Feng

"Knowing good looks means admiring young women." This sentence seems to illustrate that humans are born with an instinct to pursue love. According to research by some physiologists and psychologists, this instinct is stronger than any other instinct. Although the urge to love is inherent in everyone, it is extremely difficult for us to achieve the purpose of seeking love and find an object that suits our ideal! Therefore, I want to talk about my ideal lover: At the same time, I hope female compatriots will also talk about the objects they require.

Now let's talk about a few kinds of women I'm familiar with. I think Japanese women do have a graceful and moving figure and a gentle and melodious tone, but their semi-barbaric clothing, especially their cow-like waddling gait, is really unbearable; at the same time, their slave-like obedience to their husbands also makes me feel inexplicably uncomfortable. The idea of a virtuous wife and loving mother is not bad, but I always feel that it is interesting for both men and women to obey and love each other. If men are respected like gods by women like Japanese women, it will inevitably make people feel bored. As for French women, their appearance, their dress, their behavior and speech are all impeccable, but according to my intuition, among the three kinds of women I have the most contact with, namely German, French, and Japanese, German women best meet my ideal: they have strong bodies, sincere and passionate feelings, diligent and hard-working spirits, and awareness of serving society. If someone wants me to choose one of the three kinds of women, German, French, and Japanese, I will not hesitate to choose German women. However, since I am Chinese, my ideal lover must of course be a Chinese woman.

Because I spend very little time in the country, I have very few opportunities to contact domestic women, so I don’t know much about their qualities. On the surface, Chinese women seem to have made some progress recently, but most of their decorations are unbearably vulgar, and most of their expressions make people nauseous. At the same time, many modern women seem to regard work as a kind of shame, and everyone only knows how to spend money, play mahjong, watch movies, dance...etc. As for what is called society, country, and the value and meaning of life, they simply don't know or want to know. In fact, this kind of woman is worthless. However, in such a big country as China, I absolutely do not believe that I cannot find an ideal woman. I now try to set a standard as follows: 1. Have a healthy body. 2. Have a gentle personality. 3. Have thrifty habits. 4. Do not admire vanity. 5. Do not play mahjong. 6. Do not participate in the political activities of "political parties". 7. Have something in common with me. My standard is really not harsh at all, but since I returned to China, I have not met such a woman!

The Luo of Yunnan (III) 282

— Wang Yu

They gathered together, arranged in a chaotic line. Those who beat the gongs beat the gongs, those who knocked the shovels knocked the shovels. Men and women mixed together, talking and laughing, joyfully moving along the country lanes like a long snake towards the river. When they arrived at the river, everyone walked barefoot into the water, filled each person's bowl with clean, fine sand, and then inserted the flowers in each person's hand above the bowl of sand. Returning to the Burmese temple. Everyone pushed the collected sand into the yard and piled it up into a small mountain, and also inserted a part of each person's flowers on this sand pile. People who could dance danced around the sand pile, and those who couldn't dance watched from the side. The sound of music shook the sky, and they dispersed only when it was dusk.

Thereafter, every day was like this, and the pile of sand in the yard grew higher and higher.

It was even more lively during the grand harvesting. On this day, people from several villages gathered together, each person still having a bowl of sand and a bunch of flowers. They paraded from this village to that village, from this Burmese temple to that Burmese temple, the sound of gongs and drums was even louder, and some people even wore strange masks and danced along the way. On this day, many glutinous rice meals were prepared in each village. This was prepared for people to eat. If we ran to visit, we could also get a group.

Their glutinous rice meals are all dyed golden yellow with the flowers of a certain plant, and they have a delicious fragrance when eaten.

At night, many fireworks are set off in the Burmese temple. Their fireworks are made by putting some gunpowder and iron filings in a person's bamboo tube. When released, the fireworks can fly eight zhang high, just like a towering fire tree. After the fireworks are finished, this interesting entertainment is over.

(6) Tusi Officials

The rulers of the Luo are called Tusi officials by the Han people. But among those Luo groups that are directly ruled by the Han people, there are no more Tusi officials.

The Tusi official is like an ancient chieftain. He owns some land, and he can seal off a part of the land to his sons or relatives. In his territory, he has the power to control everything. He can obtain what he requests from the people without paying a penny - whether it is a good-walking horse or a beautiful girl.

The Luo people only have absolute obedience to their Tusi. When meeting the Tusi, they must kowtow. Moreover, when the Tusi does not tell him to stand up or squat down, he must kneel on the ground all the time.

However, the Tusi officials must also kowtow to the Grand Buddha when he sees the Grand Buddha.

(7) Their Marriage

I don't know very much about their marriage, which I feel very ashamed of and very sorry to the readers. However, I can tell you this: the relationship between men and women is very free among the Luo. Many grandmothers and mothers often say to their shy grandchildren: "Go play with the little girl." It can be said that the concept of chastity is very weak in their minds - perhaps completely absent. However, those Luo who live with the Han people have already picked up some hypocritical colors from the Han society.

Brides are usually married off at dawn. They do not sit in sedan chairs, but are led running by two women in the crowd. However, the bride must not walk across the bridge herself. When crossing the bridge, she must be carried by someone.

On the wedding night, there is an entertainment called "hitting songs". This is probably the same nature as the "teasing the bridal chamber" that is very popular in Han society.

On the first night, several square tables are arranged in the yard, and a large wine bottle and many drinking bowls or cups are placed on the tables. Several incense sticks are also lit on the tables. Men and women, everyone gathers around the table, eating wine, singing, and dancing around these square tables. They advance three steps and retreat three steps, sometimes dancing in a circle, sometimes holding hands together to dance. This is how "hitting songs" begins, and it must be played all night or even all night long.

(8) Their Future

The facts tell us that some Luo are serving as military officers in military camps (some are serving as regimental commanders), some Luo have graduated from normal schools and are serving as elementary school teachers, and many Luo children can only speak Mandarin and cannot speak Luo. Many Luo customs have been abandoned, and many Han customs have been adopted by them. In short, they are imitating the Han people everywhere. When you say they are Luo, they will think you are deliberately insulting them, and they will fight with you. Judging from these places, we can already prove that these Luo are gradually being assimilated. At the same time, this also indicates our mission - to educate them and lead them!

Long Creative Writing

The Crossroads of the Times and Love XIV 283

— Zhang Ziping

"Schoolwork is too busy, and I'm afraid I won't have many opportunities to write articles in the future, so let's organize the old manuscripts first."

He had just opened the book title, took out the physics, chemistry, and advanced algebra textbooks and three or four notebooks, and after sorting them out, he took out the essays he had written in the past from the drawer.

He heard footsteps outside the door. He thought Mrs. Tsuruko was coming up to talk to him. Because he and she had gotten into this habit, he felt extremely lonely if he didn't meet and chat about worldly gossip for one evening, as if he had a wish unfulfilled.

But the amah came in, carrying a pot of boiling water.

"Want to change the tea leaves?"

The amah's voice had no beauty whatsoever.

"No need."

Because it wasn't Mrs. Tsuruko who came up, he was a little disappointed, so he casually answered the amah. He felt in his heart that Mrs. Tsuruko was too hateful, not coming up to see him for so long. At the same time, he became angry at that Japanese man.

"If it weren't for the two female guests downstairs, I would really take that baseball bat and beat that old Japanese devil."

The more he thought about it, the angrier he became. He wanted Mrs. Tsuruko to come up quickly and explain it to him so he could calm down. But using force against the Japanese was just an ideal. When the Japanese got fierce, the Chinese didn't dare to resist at all.

"In case I start a fight and cause a diplomatic problem, that would be terrible. Forget it."

Haiquan became timid again. Although he was flipping through his old manuscripts, he not only had no intention of organizing them, he didn't even want to read them. He was really unable to get over his anger at Mrs. Tsuruko; once she had a Japanese friend, she neglected him.

He sat at his desk, daydreaming for more than two hours, becoming more and more impatient. In the end, he walked to the stairwell and listened with his ear pressed to the floor below. Those Japanese guests still hadn't left, and there was another burst of very happy laughter.

"This is really outrageous!"

Haiquan thought, wasn't this deliberately mocking his loneliness?

He walked back to his desk, feeling an indescribable sadness in his heart. He himself didn't know why he was so angry tonight.

"There are analytical geometry exercises tomorrow, and no matter what, I'm in no mood to calculate them tonight. Tomorrow, when the teacher calls me up, I'll just say I caught a cold and didn't prepare to calculate them."

So he thought of Zhuo Shuhua that he had seen this morning. From Zhuo Shuhua, he was linked to Mrs. Ren, and from Mrs. Ren, he thought of Miss Peizhu in the South.

He heard someone coming up from below again. It was indeed Mrs. Tsuruko. Haiquan was a little angry and couldn't greet her at the door like he usually did.

"Mr. Lin!"

Opinion

Even Confucius and Mencius Have Become Puppets of Puppets 284

— Buddhist

A gentleman came to Shanghai from Shenyang the other day. According to him, after the Japanese forcibly occupied the Northeast, in addition to vigorously invading in politics and economy, their cultural aggression policy is particularly alarming. They stipulate that the Four Books must be a compulsory course in all schools, etc. Confucius and Mencius are truly two strange creatures of our country. When they were alive, they spoke of benevolence and righteousness to the states of the Zhou Dynasty, but no one believed them. Once they died, suddenly "their doctrine flourished greatly." Not only do our country's ambitious people hang their golden signboard to sell fake medicine, anesthetizing countless heroes and burying countless good men, but now even the puppet state organized by the Japanese also hangs their golden signboard. Aren't Confucius and Mencius becoming puppets of puppets? I can't help but feel wronged for the two gentlemen.

The doctrine of Confucius takes respecting the Zhou Dynasty and "repelling the barbarians" as its purpose, and the sayings of Mencius take advocating benevolence and righteousness and "rejecting military force" as its purpose. Now they insist on pulling Confucius and Mencius to be teachers of Northeast youth, which is really "scolding the monk while facing the Buddha," and can be regarded as "prescribing the right medicine." Wang Mang of the Han Dynasty, secretly harboring different ambitions, opened his mouth with Yao and Shun, and closed his mouth with Zhou and Confucius. Every move was based on ancient times and the so-called former kings. After the decision, the treacherous schemes were fully revealed. Everything in the past was mostly false. As a result, the golden signboard was smashed, and the deceptive means ultimately failed.

Japanese people! Puppets! This kind of policy of fooling the people has long passed, and it is no longer applicable to the modern trend. Our country has already put the Four Books and Five Classics on a high shelf. Only a very small number of schools still use the Four Books as teaching materials for research. Now Japan wants to use this magic weapon to tightly control and anesthetize the youth of the three provinces. This is truly a dream within a dream. I am afraid that the youth of the three provinces will not be utilized by you. Confucius and Mencius will also not be loyal to you. It can be seen that the Japanese still have "Tang Dynasty-ized" minds, and this kind of trick is quite ridiculous.

Do the Japanese really want to know the theories of Confucius and Mencius? I will point out a few words of Mencius for you to listen to.

Mencius said, "Then the king's great desire can be known. He desires to expand the territory, pay court to Qin and Chu, rule China, and pacify the four barbarians. To seek what you desire by doing what you do is like climbing a tree to catch fish. Although you cannot catch fish by climbing a tree, there will be no subsequent disasters. To seek what you desire by doing what you do, and to do it with all your heart and strength, there will surely be disasters."

He also said, "Killing a Yue person for goods, fearing not death, all the people will resent it. This is to be punished without teaching."

Scientific Vegetable Fragrant Oil 285

— Qiuxin

Many plants contain fragrant oil. This type of fragrant oil is often contained in one part of the plant, such as flowers, leaves, roots, etc., and is mostly used to make cosmetics, because the fragrance of artificial fragrances is ultimately not as elegant and fresh as natural fragrances. Our country uses a lot, but unfortunately, the only domestic product is mint oil.

To extract fragrant oil, first, you must know which part contains the oil:

㈠ Flower fragrant oils are mostly contained in petals. Such as rose, jasmine, honeysuckle, orange blossom, lilac, magnolia, large lavender, violet, etc.

㈡ Leaves that contain fragrant oil include mint leaves, eucalyptus leaves, fragrant grass leaves, wintergreen leaves, laurel leaves, birch leaves, etc.

㈢ Wood and bark sandalwood, camphor tree wood, cedar tree wood, etc.; oil is contained in the bark, such as cinnamon bark.

㈣ Roots and rhizomes angelica root, camphor root, chestnut root, those contained in rhizomes include alfalfa, iris, etc.

㈤ Fruits ripe fruits contain fragrant oil, such as lemon, bergamot, orange, etc.

㈥ Seeds cloves, fennel, bitter almonds, etc.

The method of extracting fragrant oil varies depending on the situation, there are several types:

(1) Pressing method This method is mostly used for fruits. Press the mature fruit peel in a press, and filter the resulting oil with gauze or cotton to obtain it. This method can only be used for plants with a large amount of oil content because it cannot be fully squeezed out.

(2) Maceration method Cut the oil-containing part of the plant into pieces and macerate it in oil or grease. The fragrant oil is then extracted. To a considerable concentration, dissolve it with alcohol, and then evaporate the alcohol to obtain a thick fragrant oil.

Or use a volatile solvent (such as ether, de-ether, carbon tetrachloride, etc.) to pass it through layers of petals (or one part of other plants), then the fragrant oil is completely dissolved by the solvent, and then use evaporation to remove the solvent to obtain it. But it often contains resin, pigment and wax that fall into the volatile solvent.

(3) Distillation method Place the oil-containing plant or part of it in water and distill it: the fragrant oil comes out with the steam. Because water and oil cannot be mixed, remove the water from the resulting milky liquid with a separatory funnel to obtain it. The oil obtained by this method often has a burnt smell because the plant body is easily adhered to the bottom of the pot and burned by the fire.

(4) Steam distillation method The principle of this method is the same as the distillation method, but instead of directly burning with flames, steam is used. That is, the steam emitted from a steam boiler passes through a distiller containing the plant body. The oil obtained by this method is often different from the original aroma of the plant. Because some fragrant oils have a high boiling point and cannot come out with the steam: some are also decomposed by heat: therefore, it is often impossible to obtain the same fragrance as the original plant.

Good fragrant oil is colorless. Has volatility. Each has a special aroma. Easily flows. Its specific gravity is between 0.84 and 0.87. (Cinnamon and clove oil are heavier than water)

Fragrant oil is often exposed to sunlight and can gradually turn yellow or brown. More contact with air, chlorinated, becomes a viscous, difficult-to-flow substance. All fragrant oils have the ability to prevent decay. Some are also used for medicinal purposes, such as mint oil, cinnamon oil, etc.

Public English in the Office 286

Years of continuous civil war, coupled with the decline of the world economy, and the skin-cutting pain of September 18th and January 28th, how could the Shanghai market not decline to the extreme! Look at the flags of big sales and big auctions all over the street, blowing their own horns, all they want is to attract some customers, right?

There are usually a lot of clerks in this office: in three rooms, there are at least seventeen or eight people sitting, some typing, some calculating accounts, some drawing blueprints, and a lot of idle talk. This year is not right: business is too slow, income is sharply reduced, and capitalists (Westerners) have to implement a tightening policy, and have successively laid off more than a dozen employees, leaving only a few indispensable key figures.

"My pen hasn't moved today, and I can go home in another hour," said Lao Wang.

Lao Zhang chewed peanuts and said: "There's nothing to do, but there's no way: come, come, let's play a game of chess, okay?"

So Lao Wang and Lao Zhang started a chess battle.

Lao Tao put his hands in his trousers pockets, swayed back and forth, and ran in from the factory: squinting with his nearsighted eyes, watching Lao Wang and Lao Zhang's chess game; while muttering to Lao Zhou, "Lao Zhou, I can finish your Tales of Jianghu Knights tomorrow, lend me a better book."

Lao Zhou ate watermelon seeds, holding a Dream of the Red Chamber and watching it with great absorption, replied, "There are no more books, you can read this Dream of the Red Chamber."

Suddenly, there was a shout and chase outside. It turned out that Lao Sun left a love letter on the table while watching chess: Lao Xu took it. When Lao Sun found out, he rushed to fight with Lao Xu. Just when it was about to become uncontrollable, the car arrived outside. The sound of the car door closing immediately made the unrestrained members of the office return to their seats. There was silence.

Lao Wang whispered, "Damn it! What is he doing here again in five minutes?"

How to Prepare to Go to the Countryside 287

Editor:

Isn't the most popular slogan now, besides "Resisting Japan and Saving the Country," chanting "Go to the Countryside"? But, trying to explore the effect, I am afraid that it will not attract many young people to do it in a down-to-earth manner. Of course, one reason is that the prosperous city has bewitched the hearts of the entire youth, making them unwilling to explore the desolate countryside; but I think, society does not give a concrete way, so that young people have something to follow, it is not a major reason. For example, like me, it is mostly because of this reason, and economic pressure, lack of knowledge, make my usual dream of "going to the countryside," especially engaging in "rural cooperative undertakings," has always become an ideal, and still be a clerk in a company, so sir! I want to ask you to answer the following two questions:

㈠ Are there any places in society that provide free training for rural cooperative talents? And please introduce its content.

㈡ If not, what transitional methods should be used to achieve the goal?

Goodbye! Wishing you health! (Guo Ding'an)

Editor's note: Since the Industrial Revolution, whether in Britain or the United States, a large number of farmers have had to abandon their original fields and run to the cities. These people can be said to have been grabbed from the countryside to the city by machines. As a result, the urbanization of cities and the anemia-like desolation of rural areas have progressed with the times. This is a tragedy that has been playing out in Europe for a long time; and now? It is even more bitter that a large number of unemployed workers want to return to the countryside but cannot.

Unfortunately, China, which feels backward in everything, is decades late in staging the old tricks of others, which is really a tragic and sad phenomenon. International capital imperialism has long formed a united front. In addition to implementing vicious economic aggression, it also takes advantage of the opportunity to stir up continuous infighting among warlords in your country. Ordinary farmers want to come to the city to be slaves to machines but cannot, and can only turn into cannon fodder or starved corpses.

Shanghai, known as the Paris of the East, is a cursed market. It is the base camp for imperialist aggression against China. Its development is irrigated with the blood and tears of the people of the whole country. Everything is building, everything is equipped, and everything is being Europeanized. Who is not tempted by this intoxicating place? Who still has the perseverance to go to the "desolate countryside"? People who "chant to go to the countryside" are just using the slogan as a signboard, and they still want to sit in cars and circle on asphalt roads, right? Shanghai, I am afraid, has become a cradle that the majority of people absolutely cannot leave. Although "going to the countryside," "relieving the countryside," and "transforming the countryside" ... are currently serious problems recognized by everyone.

Guo Ding'an is a clerk in a company, and he actually wants to realize the slogan "go to the countryside," which cannot but be regarded as a young man with a unique vision. Regarding the two questions raised: First, the school for training rural cooperative talents; as far as the editor knows, there is none yet. Regarding the second question, we have the following opinions to provide to Guo Jun for reference.

㈠ Please read books on rural cooperation first;

㈡ Go to people who have studied rural cooperation for advice; (such as Mr. Wang Zhixin, manager of Xinhua Bank, etc.)

㈢ Go to the model village run by the China Vocational Education Society (in Xugongqiao) for on-site observation.

The editor is aware of his shallow knowledge and limited experience, so he also puts forward this question to ask everyone to express their opinions. The three previous questions are all written below:

㈠ Standing in the position of a clerk, worker, or apprentice, how can we fulfill the obligations of a member of the Republic of China to resist Japan and save the country?

㈡ How can clerks, apprentices, or trainees satisfy their desire for knowledge?

㈢ Standing in the position of a clerk, what methods should be used to engage in communication and improve living conditions?

㈣ Standing in the position of a clerk, what methods should be used to realize the slogan "go to the countryside"?

Novel

Writing a Letter to a Friend's Wife (Continued 6) 288

— Qin Shouou

But after I washed my face and felt a little clearer, I decided that I must leave. Why is that?

Do you remember, beautiful little pig! Last spring, didn't I disappear for more than a month? Later, in the winter, didn't I also have a gap of forty or fifty days with you? Let me tell you the truth! These two times were both sacrifices and failures of my preparation to endure the pain and break up with you. The so-called going to the Nanjing Judicial Yuan and the Hangzhou Education Department are really all lies!

The first time in the spring, I gradually discovered the pain after Da Jing lost your love. He was originally an unfortunate person who had already lost his love, and he had been so decadent like an old man over sixty years old because of that loss of love; on average, it was not easy to see a smile once every ten days; he lived this tomb-like life for as long as four years. It was not until the end of the year before last, when your little rose was born, that he gradually regained his youthful vitality like a withered tree in spring.

I am his old friend and old classmate. Of course, I am very happy and extremely pleased with the revival of his soul; unfortunately, at the same time, I fell in love with you. Originally, love can only be given to one person: I loved you, so I forgot all the people in the family: you accepted my love, and naturally, you also had some perversions towards Da Jing. This kind of perversion can deceive an ordinary person, but it cannot deceive Zhou Da Jing, whose thoughts are as profound as mine. So he became lifeless again.

One day, he was sick, he was suffering from stomach disease; but he did not drink medicine, but ate and drank a lot of greasy things with cold water. This one shadow character is sharper than a sharp knife, and immediately stabbed a big hole in my heart. The second time, I decided to abandon you.

Although my body did not come to your house, my heart could not forget you. I would even think of you every minute.

"This is not good!" I also felt that if I kept thinking about you all the time, sooner or later, I would repeat my return to you: so I tried my best to plan to drive that ivory snake-like figure out of my brain. After planning for a long time, I finally found a way out. What is that? It is "whoring"!

Whoring was also a common occurrence for me before. When I was studying at the 口Da Middle School, I was already an old customer in the Xiaohuayuan and Huileli areas. To put it bluntly, my dormitory at that time was set up in Huileli, Xiaohuayuan.

Lovely little friend! Little brother! Didn't you often force me to tell you about whoring before? However, at that time, because you were obviously not discussing whoring with me in order to approve of my whoring: you were satirizing me. So I was not willing to tell the truth, so as not to make you angry. But, now, I have been taken by the Tianjin-Pukou Railway to thousands of miles away from you: and in fact, I am not allowed to see you again in my lifetime; even if you hate me and despise me, I cannot hope to be affected in any way! Then, should I definitely hide my sins! Okay! Let me tell you something about whoring!

Although I am also a woman, you are noble and happy women, how can you think of the pain of those prostitutes who sit in silk cars and wear new clothes! Their place of residence is called Tangzi in Shanghai; according to your thoughts, Tangzi must be a paradise, a place of pleasure. In fact, they are all ten-foot-long powder hells! They try their best to decorate themselves in hell, waiting for a group of men who have nowhere to vent their desires and nowhere to vent their anger to vent their anger.

I used to belong to the first two categories: last spring, I belonged to the second category!

However, whoring in Shanghai has a difficulty, that is, it cannot be without a partner; when I was madly whoring at the beginning, there were no less than thirteen or fourteen people. Everyone was closer than their own brothers, mixed together every day, and it was easy to whoring at any time and anywhere; later, it suddenly ended, and in a blink of an eye, three years have passed. Now if I want to whoring again, I have no partner! It was easy for me to find a few flower-filled and wine-loving friends who volunteered to join the group.

Movie Special Issue

Overseas News

"Paramount's" Shanghai War Film 289

— Meilang

...Total profit of more than 2.4 million...

In the Battle of Shanghai, Chinese and Western film companies competed to carry the "camera" to the battlefield to film the war. There were many types of films. At the beginning of the war, the Shanghai-based cameramen of the American "Paramount" and "Fox" companies sent the war newsreels they had filmed as soon as possible. For fear of falling behind, the competition between the two sides was very fierce.

At that time, the films of the two companies were sent from Shanghai on the "President McKinley" at the same time. After completing the film mailing procedures, both parties sent telegrams to notify their respective companies of the facts and requested that they be picked up quickly.

After receiving this message, "Paramount" agreed with the naval authorities and borrowed a seaplane from the nearby fleet to fly to the mooring surface of "Honolulu" to wait. When the "McKinley" came roaring, it immediately attached to the wheel and climbed up, extracted the film and drove the plane to fly to New York.

"Paramount" took comprehensive considerations into account. From "Honolulu" to "New York," a distance of thousands of miles, it also sent two planes to wait in advance at two points with considerable distance. They took turns flying. After such careful arrangement, it arrived first. On the day of the premiere, it was a sensation, and the business was very prosperous. Although "Fox" also used other methods of rapid transportation to try to win, it was already nine hours late.

Recently, people from Paramount said, "Regarding the settlement of the business accounts of this Shanghai war film, the profit was more than 2.4 million."

Betty Lawford, like other female stars in Hollywood, often covers her eyes with her hair. She says that the silver lights on the set are too strong, so she has to protect them a little with her hair. Of course, it would be better to cover her eyes completely, but the facts do not allow it. She is the pearl of famous actor Ernest Lawford. Since starring in The Monkey's Paw, she has become the star of stars.

Fragments of Film World Gossip

(1) Jin Yan's Patriotic Heart 290

— Sen

After the September 18th National Crisis, the people of the country were very angry, and Jin Yan was even more angry, because he was originally a Korean, so he was more concerned about the rise and fall of his homeland! He was more anxious than any Chinese, wishing to immediately recover the Northeast occupied by the Japanese, even though he had no home in the Northeast at that time.

At that time, the emerging theater troupes in Shanghai were surging. There were troupes with the broad goal of anti-imperialism, and troupes with the narrow goal of patriotism. To put it simply, there were only these two types. The Northeast Shanghai Fellow Countrymen's Anti-Japanese Association was preparing to organize a theater troupe and invited Jin Yan to participate. At that time, he agreed with great enthusiasm and said, "This is my personal duty, and of course I cannot refuse." The script selected was "On the Banks of the Yinma River," with Jin Yan as the protagonist. It was prepared to be performed at sea.

Although the play was not performed at that time, it was known how indignant Jin Yan was about the national crisis.

(2) Ruan Lingyu's Face 291

— Sen

A few days ago, I accidentally turned out an old newspaper and saw a passage about the Chinese movie queen Ruan Lingyu. The passage said that Ruan Lingyu's charm, enthusiasm, and beauty were indeed no less than Clara Bow's, but the only shortcoming was that she had some shallow pockmarks on her face recently. It did not hinder filming with the camera, but it was actually not hidden, which was a pity. That's roughly what it meant, because that newspaper is no longer in my hands.

I have seen Ruan Lingyu before, and I have seen her recently, and it seems that there are no pockmarks on her face. So, what's going on?

If Ruan Lingyu has some fine spots on her face, this is inevitable. However, spots can be completely concealed by decorative techniques when they are young. But now that Ruan Lingyu is not too old, and she does not lack decoration, I am afraid that the spots on her face are not easily seen by outsiders. As for saying that Ruan Lingyu has pockmarks on her face, I do not quite agree with this, because pockmarks are absolutely different from spots.

A Short History of Movie Stars

Ai Xia 292

— Xia

Ms. Ai Xia is a rising star among the stars; she was born in Beiping; but her ancestral home is Hebei. Many people mistakenly think that she is from Beiping, but that is a misunderstanding.

She is very talented and intelligent. At the age of seventeen, she studied at the Sacred Heart Girls' Middle School in Beiping. She is gentle and amiable, so her classmates are very friendly to her.

She has been fond of drama since she was a child. In her spare time, she especially likes to read drama books. When she has a book in hand, she has the idea of "forgetting to eat and sleep." Later, for some reason, she transferred to another school; after graduation, she established a drama troupe in Beiping. Most of the scripts were written by herself. At that time, she received a warm welcome from the local people; later, the actors dispersed, and it finally disbanded.

In the spring of the 19th year, she came to Shanghai. In response to the invitation of the Nanguo Drama Society, she joined the troupe as a member; once she performed in the play "Father Returns" on a certain stage. She played the lead role and won a lot of praise. But she was not satisfied; she wanted to pursue further studies, and she did intermittent research at Xinhua University of the Arts; a year later, she left Nanguo and entered Tianyi Company through the introduction of her friend; in October of this year. She was transferred from Dayi Company to Mingxing Company; "Old Hatreds and New Sorrows," which was recently premiered in the Central, is her debut work.

Secrets of the Film World: A Mysterious Hollywood Duo – Xiao Yu 294

Since the film "Morocco" became popular, Ms. Garbo's mystique seems to have lost its unique appeal.

In the two years since Marlene Dietrich arrived in Hollywood, she has achieved success with five masterpieces, bringing extraordinary brilliance to the film industry.

Some say that Dietrich's style is somewhat like Garbo's. This statement seems credible, yet one cannot fully believe it. It is only that the expressions of both have reached perfection.

Furthermore, Garbo and Dietrich not only share similar styles and reputations, but their histories of entering the film industry, and their relationships with directors, are also somewhat similar. At the age of sixteen, Garbo met her director Stiller in Sweden. He persuaded Garbo to join the film world, brought her to Hollywood, guided her, and admired her. Von Sternberg met Dietrich in Germany; similarly, he brought her to America, directed her, and supported her.

Upon arriving in a foreign land, both Garbo and Dietrich felt unfamiliar and lonely. Only the directors who accompanied them day and night were there to protect them. Perhaps it was because their relationships with their respective directors were too close, or perhaps they felt grateful for the painstaking efforts of these two great directors in nurturing them, and wanted to repay their kindness. The Creation and Development of Animated Cartoons 295

— Mei Cun

Walt Disney was a clever and young, poor artist. Not long after the end of the European War, he was an employee at a commercial art studio in Kansas City. He often drew advertisements for an agricultural magazine, giving him a thorough understanding of various animals. Sometimes he had to continue working late into the night, so he often prepared snacks in a paper box to satisfy his hunger when he was hungry. At midnight, groups of mice would sneak into the paper box to steal snacks. He found their leaping movements interesting and drew sketches of their dance, which he later published in the magazine and were well-received by readers. After some experimentation, it was filmed and put on the screen.

Four years ago, a 丨丨ＭｏｉｃｄｅｙＭｏｕｃｅ company was established in Hollywood, dedicated to the work of animated cartoons. Now, the company's business is booming, with over three hundred employees. There are also more than sixty artisans who manufacture various toys. According to a recent survey in the United States, there are 300,000 small stores that retail these toys; 172 newspapers carry advertisements for these animated films; and over 15,000 theaters show these films. If a worldwide survey were conducted, the results would be even more astonishing!

News About Crying Bitterly from Film Monographs 296

— Chen Dabei

The habit of freely shedding tears may be considered difficult to cultivate by the British and Americans. Because after leaving infancy, they may still have the opportunity to shed tears, but it is very difficult for men to do so. It is not the same for us Chinese. As long as one is not heartbroken or insane, can one not find one or two news items in the daily newspaper that can move you to tears?

Using these tragic reports to elicit your tears is probably easy. This is certainly not the proper method. Because pursuers of art should be rich in emotion. Those rich in emotion, when practicing expressions alone, only need the assistance of the mind and breathing to surely develop the ability to cry genuinely.

Now we are going to practice the eighth style of expression self-study. The student first stands upright facing a mirror. While silently counting "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight," slowly inhale a breath of air through the nostrils, gradually focusing the gaze on sadness, gradually frowning, and gradually lowering the corners of the lips, transforming into a crying face.

Maintain this crying face while silently counting "one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight." After counting these eight words, then slowly exhale this breath of air through the nostrils. When the degree of crying progresses to the extreme, the heartache and tears that fall will be almost identical to genuine crying. The only difference is that genuine crying is not under your control. This kind of crying expression that resembles genuine crying is completely under your control.
